[[Source]](https://starwars.fandom.com/wiki/Template:Organization)

:   "*Well, I've known no other way. Gives us clones all a mixed feeling about the war. Many people wish it never happened. But without it, we clones wouldn't exist.*"
:   ―Rex, on being a clone trooper[[9]](#cite_note-Shattered-9)

**Clone troopers**, also known as **Clone soldiers**, **Republic troopers**, **Republic troops**, **Republic soldiers**, **Regs**, and nicknamed the "**Boys in White**," were highly trained [soldiers](/wiki/Soldier "Soldier") in the [Grand Army of the Republic](/wiki/Grand_Army_of_the_Republic "Grand Army of the Republic"). Representing the future of [galactic](/wiki/Galaxy "Galaxy") warfare, [clones](/wiki/Cloning "Cloning") were designed to be far superior to [battle droids](/wiki/Battle_droid "Battle droid"). During the [last years](/wiki/Republic_Era "Republic Era") of the [Galactic Republic](/wiki/Galactic_Republic "Galactic Republic"), clones formed the backbone of the [Republic Military](/wiki/Republic_Military "Republic Military"), which waged war against the [droid armies](/wiki/Separatist_Droid_Army "Separatist Droid Army") of the [Confederacy of Independent Systems](/wiki/Confederacy_of_Independent_Systems "Confederacy of Independent Systems"). The [Clone Wars](/wiki/Clone_Wars "Clone Wars") were named after the Republic's clone [army](/wiki/Army "Army"), which became symbolic of the conflict that had spread throughout [the galaxy](/wiki/The_galaxy "The galaxy") after a [millennium](/wiki/Millennium "Millennium") of [peace](/wiki/Republic_Era "Republic Era").

Clone [troopers](/wiki/Trooper "Trooper") were grown on the [planet](/wiki/Planet "Planet") [Kamino](/wiki/Kamino "Kamino") at the request of [Jedi Master](/wiki/Jedi_Master "Jedi Master") [Sifo-Dyas](/wiki/Sifo-Dyas "Sifo-Dyas"), who commissioned the [Kaminoans](/wiki/Kaminoan "Kaminoan") to build an army for the Republic. After Sifo Dyas' [death](/wiki/Death "Death"), the project was taken over by the [Sith](/wiki/Sith "Sith"). Clones were modeled on a [human](/wiki/Human "Human") [template](/wiki/Clone_template "Clone template"), the [Mandalorian](/wiki/Mandalorian "Mandalorian") [bounty hunter](/wiki/Bounty_hunter "Bounty hunter") [Jango Fett](/wiki/Jango_Fett "Jango Fett"), although their [genetic structure](/wiki/DNA "DNA") was modified to make them less independent and more docile than their progenitor. They were also designed to age at twice the rate of [natural](/wiki/Reproduction "Reproduction") humans, accelerating their growth and making them ready for combat in a [decade's](/wiki/Standard_decade "Standard decade") [time](/wiki/Time "Time"). As the [Separatist Crisis](/wiki/Separatist_Crisis "Separatist Crisis") gave way to open war, the [Galactic Senate](/wiki/Galactic_Senate "Galactic Senate") empowered [Supreme Chancellor](/wiki/Supreme_Chancellor "Supreme Chancellor") [Sheev Palpatine](/wiki/Darth_Sidious "Darth Sidious") to call the clone troopers into action, leading to their debut on the [battlefield](/wiki/First_Battle_of_Geonosis "First Battle of Geonosis") of [Geonosis](/wiki/Geonosis "Geonosis"). For three [years](/wiki/Standard_year "Standard year"), clones fought the Separatist [droids](/wiki/Droid "Droid") on all fronts across the galaxy. They were loyal to their [Jedi Generals](/wiki/Jedi_General "Jedi General") and the Supreme Chancellor; though some clones questioned their service, leading to isolated cases of [desertion](/wiki/Cut_Lawquane "Cut Lawquane") and [treason](/wiki/Slick "Slick"), most were proud to serve the Republic as it was the only life they had ever known.

[Galactic history](/wiki/Timeline_of_galactic_history "Timeline of galactic history") was forever changed by a hidden [behavioral modification biochip](/wiki/Behavioral_modification_biochip "Behavioral modification biochip") implanted in every clone, which was part of the Sith's plot to destroy the Jedi. Chancellor Palpatine, [discovered](/wiki/Duel_in_Palpatine%27s_office "Duel in Palpatine's office") by the [Jedi](/wiki/Jedi "Jedi") to be the [Sith Lord](/wiki/Sith_Lord "Sith Lord") [Darth](/wiki/Darth "Darth") Sidious, as well as the reason behind the Clone Wars, branded the Jedi as the [enemies of the state](/wiki/Treason "Treason") and issued [Order 66](/wiki/Order_66 "Order 66"), with the latter being a call for the [annihilation](/wiki/Great_Jedi_Purge "Great Jedi Purge") of the [Jedi Order](/wiki/Jedi_Order "Jedi Order"). All across the galaxy, the clones turned against their [generals](/wiki/General "General"), slaughtering them and [storming](/wiki/Operation:_Knightfall "Operation: Knightfall") the [Jedi Temple](/wiki/Imperial_Palace "Imperial Palace") on [Coruscant](/wiki/Coruscant "Coruscant") under the [stewardship](/wiki/501st_Legion "501st Legion") of the Sith [Lord](/wiki/Lord "Lord") [Darth Vader](/wiki/Anakin_Skywalker "Anakin Skywalker"). Sidious subsequently assumed [absolute power](/wiki/Dictatorship "Dictatorship") as the [self-proclaimed](/wiki/Proclamation_of_the_New_Order "Proclamation of the New Order") [Emperor](/wiki/Galactic_Emperor "Galactic Emperor") of the [Galactic Empire](/wiki/Galactic_Empire "Galactic Empire"). Clones initially served as **[Imperial stormtroopers](/wiki/Stormtrooper "Stormtrooper")** in the [New Order](/wiki/New_Order "New Order") but were [eventually](/wiki/Project_War-Mantle "Project War-Mantle") [replaced](/wiki/Imperial_Defense_Recruitment_Bill "Imperial Defense Recruitment Bill") by [birth-born human recruits and conscripts](/wiki/TK_stormtrooper "TK stormtrooper"). Their [armor](/wiki/Clone_trooper_armor "Clone trooper armor"), weapons, and training inspired generations of [armored](/wiki/Armor "Armor") warriors following on from their Imperial successors; with both the [First Order](/wiki/First_Order "First Order")'s [stormtroopers](/wiki/First_Order_stormtrooper "First Order stormtrooper") and the [Sith Eternal](/wiki/Sith_Eternal "Sith Eternal")'s [red-armored soldiers](/wiki/Sith_trooper "Sith trooper") having been [trained](/wiki/Project_Resurrection "Project Resurrection") from [early childhood](/wiki/Youngling "Youngling") to become super-soldiers much like the clone army. In particular, the latter were indoctrinated using a modified and improved upon version of the [flash-training](/wiki/Flash-training "Flash-training") techniques previously used for the clones.

## History[]

### Origin[]

:   "*They are totally obedient, taking any order without question. We modified their genetic structure to make them less independent than the original host.*"  
    "*And who was the original host?*"  
    "*A bounty hunter called Jango Fett.*"
:   ―Lama Su and Obi-Wan Kenobi[[4]](#cite_note-Episode_II-4)

[Years](/wiki/Standard_year "Standard year") before the [Invasion of Naboo](/wiki/Invasion_of_Naboo "Invasion of Naboo"), [Jedi Master](/wiki/Jedi_Master "Jedi Master") [Sifo-Dyas](/wiki/Sifo-Dyas "Sifo-Dyas") came to believe that [the galaxy](/wiki/The_galaxy "The galaxy") would soon become engulfed by war. He therefore advocated for the creation of an army to ensure the defense of the [Galactic Republic](/wiki/Galactic_Republic "Galactic Republic"), but his views were ultimately rejected by his peers and he was cast out of the [Jedi High Council](/wiki/Jedi_High_Council "Jedi High Council"). Undeterred by the lack of support from the other [Jedi](/wiki/Jedi "Jedi"), Sifo-Dyas secretly contacted the [Kaminoans](/wiki/Kaminoan "Kaminoan")[[10]](#cite_note-Sifo-Dyas-10)—a [species](/wiki/Species "Species") of experts in [cloning](/wiki/Cloning "Cloning"), native to the [planet](/wiki/Planet "Planet") [Kamino](/wiki/Kamino "Kamino")[[4]](#cite_note-Episode_II-4)—and commissioned them to create an army of clone [soldiers](/wiki/Soldier "Soldier") for the Republic without authorization from either High Council or the [Galactic Senate](/wiki/Galactic_Senate "Galactic Senate").[[10]](#cite_note-Sifo-Dyas-10) Dyas personally met with the Kaminoan [Prime Minister](/wiki/Prime_Minister "Prime Minister"), [Lama Su](/wiki/Lama_Su "Lama Su").[[11]](#cite_note-CVD-11) However, the [Sith Lord](/wiki/Sith_Lord "Sith Lord") [Darth Sidious](/wiki/Darth_Sidious "Darth Sidious") learned of Dyas' order through unknown means.[[12]](#cite_note-Creation_of_the_Clone_Army-12)

 [![Jango Fett was chosen by Sith apprentice Darth Tyranus to serve as the template for an army of clone troopers.](data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIABAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAEALAAAAAABAAEAQAICTAEAOw%3D%3D)](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/1/18/JangoFettMeetsWithDooku-AORJangoFett1.png/revision/latest?cb=20190111035238) [![Jango Fett was chosen by Sith apprentice Darth Tyranus to serve as the template for an army of clone troopers.](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/1/18/JangoFettMeetsWithDooku-AORJangoFett1.png/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/250?cb=20190111035238)](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/1/18/JangoFettMeetsWithDooku-AORJangoFett1.png/revision/latest?cb=20190111035238) 

Jango Fett was chosen by Sith apprentice Darth Tyranus to serve as the template for an army of clone troopers.

 

The [Sith apprentice](/wiki/Sith_apprentice "Sith apprentice") [Darth Tyranus](/wiki/Dooku "Dooku"), who was actually Sifo Dyas' friend and the former Jedi Master Dooku, later claimed Dyas had worked with him to create the clone army.[[13]](#cite_note-The_Lost_One-13) Shortly afterward, Sifo-Dyas was [killed](/wiki/Death "Death") by the [Pyke Syndicate](/wiki/Pyke_Syndicate "Pyke Syndicate") at the behest of the [Sith](/wiki/Sith "Sith"), resulting in the Sith's takeover of the clone trooper project.[[10]](#cite_note-Sifo-Dyas-10) Tyranus betrayed and orchestrated Sifo Dyas' death, and subsequently recruited the [Mandalorian](/wiki/Mandalorian "Mandalorian") [bounty hunter](/wiki/Bounty_hunter "Bounty hunter") [Jango Fett](/wiki/Jango_Fett "Jango Fett") to become the [genetic template](/wiki/Clone_template "Clone template") of the clone army. Various modifications were made to the Fett [genome](/wiki/DNA "DNA") so that the clones would grow faster and be more susceptible to following orders. Hyper-aggressive and volatile tendencies were tailored; the Kaminoans resorted to growth acceleration in order to create mature clones in half the [time](/wiki/Time "Time") a [human](/wiki/Human "Human") took to reach maturity. Fett's genetic structure was further modified to make the clones less independent and more docile than their template. However, the clones were also designed to be capable of creative thinking,[[4]](#cite_note-Episode_II-4) making them far superior to [battle droids](/wiki/Battle_droid "Battle droid").[[1]](#cite_note-clonetroopers-1) After being created on Kamino,[[14]](#cite_note-Ultimate_Star_Wars_New-14) some clones were secretly raised on [Coruscant](/wiki/Coruscant "Coruscant") to become the [shock troopers](/wiki/Imperial_shock_trooper "Imperial shock trooper") of the [Coruscant Guard](/wiki/Coruscant_Guard "Coruscant Guard").[[11]](#cite_note-CVD-11) Fett became a near-mythologized figure to his clones, who regarded him as their father figure.[[15]](#cite_note-Rise-15) Fett himself, however, did not feel a sense of pride in his clones, instead seeing them as "livestock" made to be "cannon fodder." As such, he considered them to be the Kaminoans' creations instead of his.[[16]](#cite_note-Age_of_Republic_Jango-16)

Fett was paid a considerable amount of [credits](/wiki/Galactic_Credit_Standard "Galactic Credit Standard")[[4]](#cite_note-Episode_II-4) for allowing the Kaminoans to use his genetic material as the clone army's template;[[17]](#cite_note-Bounty_Lost_Ep_Guide-17) his only other demand was the creation of an unaltered clone of himself, which the Kaminoans found unusual but nevertheless obliged. Whereas the clone army was genetically modified for growth acceleration and enhanced docility,[[4]](#cite_note-Episode_II-4) [Alpha](/wiki/Boba_Fett "Boba Fett")[[18]](#cite_note-Bounty_Lost-18) was an example of pure genetic replication[[4]](#cite_note-Episode_II-4) and therefore possessed pure, first generation Fett DNA.[[17]](#cite_note-Bounty_Lost_Ep_Guide-17) The only other clone like Alpha[[18]](#cite_note-Bounty_Lost-18) was an adolescent [female](/wiki/Gender "Gender") known as [Omega](/wiki/Omega "Omega").[[19]](#cite_note-Aftermath_(episode)-19) Fett took Alpha to raise as his son, renaming the clone "Boba Fett."[[4]](#cite_note-Episode_II-4) Omega remained in the custody of the Kaminoans and was serving as an [aide](/wiki/Aide "Aide")[[19]](#cite_note-Aftermath_(episode)-19) of the [Chief Medical Scientist](/wiki/Chief_Medical_Scientist "Chief Medical Scientist")[[20]](#cite_note-TCW|Conspiracy-20) [Doctor](/wiki/Doctor "Doctor") [Nala Se](/wiki/Nala_Se "Nala Se") by the end of the [Clone Wars](/wiki/Clone_Wars "Clone Wars").[[19]](#cite_note-Aftermath_(episode)-19) Like the rest of the Fett clones, they were regarded as Kaminoan property by Lama Su.[[21]](#cite_note-Replacements-21)

 [![The Sith secretly guided the creation of the clone troopers on Kamino.](data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIABAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAEALAAAAAABAAEAQAICTAEAOw%3D%3D)](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/6/69/Order66-SoH.png/revision/latest?cb=20200831141721) [![The Sith secretly guided the creation of the clone troopers on Kamino.](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/6/69/Order66-SoH.png/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/250?cb=20200831141721)](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/6/69/Order66-SoH.png/revision/latest?cb=20200831141721) 

The Sith secretly guided the creation of the clone troopers on Kamino.

 

Although the Kaminoans believed that the army was meant to serve the Republic,[[4]](#cite_note-Episode_II-4) the Sith intended to use the clone troopers as their secret weapon against the [Jedi Order](/wiki/Jedi_Order "Jedi Order"). The clone army's true purpose was to exterminate the Jedi,[[1]](#cite_note-clonetroopers-1) and to that end, an organic [inhibitor chip](/wiki/Behavioral_modification_biochip "Behavioral modification biochip") was implanted into the brain of every clone trooper at the third stage of their development. Sifo-Dyas, who had originally thought of the chip, intended for it to be a safeguard against rogue Jedi, but following his death, Sidious and Tyranus retooled the chip to ensure the Jedi's destruction. Upon the activation of the retooled chip,[[22]](#cite_note-TCW|Fugitive-22) the clones would be brainwashed[[23]](#cite_note-Journeys:_Beginnings-23) into believing that Jedi were traitors to the Republic, forcing the clones to execute the Jedi. Tyranus, who posed as a Jedi, tricked the Kaminoans into believing Sifo Dyas' intention. One chip failed in the case of [Tup](/wiki/Tup "Tup"), causing him to betray and kill a Jedi before the order was given. Officially, the chips were supposed to make the clones less aggressive and independent than Jango Fett.[[22]](#cite_note-TCW|Fugitive-22) The significance of the inhibitor chip was supported by the assertion that a clone would become mentally unstable and dangerous to everyone around him if his chip was damaged or surgically removed.[[24]](#cite_note-TCW|Orders-24) The chips were, in fact, created to compel the clone troopers to execute [Order 66](/wiki/Order_66 "Order 66")[[22]](#cite_note-TCW|Fugitive-22)[[24]](#cite_note-TCW|Orders-24)—a secret protocol that authorized the destruction of the Jedi Order.[[2]](#cite_note-Episode_III-2)

 [![The clone troopers were genetically identical as a result of originating from a single source of DNA.](data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIABAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAEALAAAAAABAAEAQAICTAEAOw%3D%3D)](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/0/05/Clonestraining.jpg/revision/latest?cb=20080117183211) [![The clone troopers were genetically identical as a result of originating from a single source of DNA.](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/0/05/Clonestraining.jpg/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/250?cb=20080117183211)](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/0/05/Clonestraining.jpg/revision/latest?cb=20080117183211) 

The clone troopers were genetically identical as a result of originating from a single source of DNA.

 

Each clone trooper had an [identifying code](/wiki/Identifying_code "Identifying code") inserted in his left wrist. During the Clone Wars, the codes were linked to the file of every individual trooper in the Republic's military database. The files, which could be accessed by an [astromech droid](/wiki/Astromech_droid "Astromech droid") via the scanning of a clone's identifying code, contained the clones' designation, rank and overall service record, as well as any specialized training and the units that he was affiliated with.[[25]](#cite_note-Missing_in_Action-25) Most clones also shared their template's [dark-brown](/wiki/Color "Color") [eyes](/wiki/Eye "Eye"), black [hair](/wiki/Hair "Hair"), and olive skin. While there were some genetic variations, most of these clones would ultimately remain confined to Kamino, being embarrassments or case studies.[[15]](#cite_note-Rise-15) Only five clone anomalies remained by the end of the war, including Nala Se's assistant Omega, an enhanced female clone. The other four clones formed the original lineup of [Clone Force 99](/wiki/Clone_Force_99 "Clone Force 99"). [Hunter](/wiki/Hunter "Hunter"), [Tech](/wiki/Tech "Tech"), [Wrecker](/wiki/Wrecker "Wrecker"), and [Crosshair](/wiki/Crosshair "Crosshair") were genetically enhanced clones who possessed unique combat skills, setting them apart from the standard "reg" clone troopers as well as each other.[[19]](#cite_note-Aftermath_(episode)-19)

 [![Clone Captain Rex was a generation one clone who became the hero of the entire army.](data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIABAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAEALAAAAAABAAEAQAICTAEAOw%3D%3D)](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/e/eb/RexTroopers-Agenda.png/revision/latest?cb=20091015160516) [![Clone Captain Rex was a generation one clone who became the hero of the entire army.](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/e/eb/RexTroopers-Agenda.png/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/250?cb=20091015160516)](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/e/eb/RexTroopers-Agenda.png/revision/latest?cb=20091015160516) 

Clone Captain Rex was a generation one clone who became the hero of the entire army.

 

The term "generation one" designated the first group of clones who were created from[[26]](#cite_note-Battle_Scars-26) the Jango Fett genotype,[[22]](#cite_note-TCW|Fugitive-22) including [Clone Captain](/wiki/Clone_Captain "Clone Captain") [Rex](/wiki/Rex "Rex")[[26]](#cite_note-Battle_Scars-26) of the [501st Legion](/wiki/501st_Legion "501st Legion")[[27]](#cite_note-Rex-27) and [Clone Sergeant](/wiki/Clone_Sergeant "Clone Sergeant") [Slick](/wiki/Slick "Slick").[[28]](#cite_note-lines-28) Rex's service in the Clone Wars came to make him a legend amongst the troopers, with the captain eventually being regarded as the hero of the clone army.[[29]](#cite_note-Battle_Scars_Episode_Guide_5-29) The first two-hundred thousand units were ready a decade after Sifo-Dyas commissioned the creation of the clone army. In addition to the first units, a million clones were being developed[[4]](#cite_note-Episode_II-4) in the facilities spread across Kamino[[30]](#cite_note-SWCC2016-30) at the time of [Jedi Knight](/wiki/Jedi_Knight "Jedi Knight") [Obi-Wan Kenobi](/wiki/Obi-Wan_Kenobi "Obi-Wan Kenobi")'s arrival.[[4]](#cite_note-Episode_II-4)

Kenobi discovered the clone project on Kamino and duly informed the Jedi High Council. By then, the galaxy was on the verge of a civil war between the Republic and a [secessionist movement](/wiki/Separatist_Crisis "Separatist Crisis") that ultimately formed the [Confederacy of Independent Systems](/wiki/Confederacy_of_Independent_Systems "Confederacy of Independent Systems"). Since the Jedi lacked sufficient manpower to guard the entire Republic, the Senate resolved to grant emergency powers to the executive branch. As a result, the clone troopers were formally organized into the [Grand Army of the Republic](/wiki/Grand_Army_of_the_Republic "Grand Army of the Republic") by [Supreme Chancellor](/wiki/Supreme_Chancellor "Supreme Chancellor") Sheev Palpatine[[4]](#cite_note-Episode_II-4)—the elected leader of the Senate[[2]](#cite_note-Episode_III-2) and public persona of [Darth](/wiki/Darth "Darth") Sidious, [Dark Lord of the Sith](/wiki/Dark_Lord_of_the_Sith "Dark Lord of the Sith").[[31]](#cite_note-Sith-31) With war imminent, [Grand Master](/wiki/Grand_Master "Grand Master") [Yoda](/wiki/Yoda "Yoda") traveled to Kamino to personally inspect the clone army while Jedi Master [Mace Windu](/wiki/Mace_Windu "Mace Windu") led the [vanguard](/wiki/Jedi_assault_team "Jedi assault team") against the Separatists on [Geonosis](/wiki/Geonosis "Geonosis").[[4]](#cite_note-Episode_II-4)

### Clone Wars[]

#### Soldiers of the Republic[]

:   "*I have to admit that without the clones, it would have not been a victory.*"  
    "*Victory? Victory you say? Master Obi-Wan, not victory. The shroud of the dark side has fallen. Begun the Clone War has.*"
:   ―Obi-Wan Kenobi and Yoda[[4]](#cite_note-Episode_II-4)

 [![The deployment of clone troopers marked the beginning of the Clone Wars.](data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIABAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAEALAAAAAABAAEAQAICTAEAOw%3D%3D)](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/4/42/SWL-Clone-Captain-Geonosis.png/revision/latest?cb=20210423013944) [![The deployment of clone troopers marked the beginning of the Clone Wars.](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/4/42/SWL-Clone-Captain-Geonosis.png/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/300?cb=20210423013944)](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/4/42/SWL-Clone-Captain-Geonosis.png/revision/latest?cb=20210423013944) 

The deployment of clone troopers marked the beginning of the Clone Wars.

 

Clone troopers were deployed into battle for the first time on the planet Geonosis, where twelve [*Acclamator*-class assault ships](/wiki/Acclamator-class_transgalactic_military_assault_ship "Acclamator-class transgalactic military assault ship") supplied by Kamino were loaded with two battle armies,[[15]](#cite_note-Rise-15) or 192,000 troops.[[30]](#cite_note-SWCC2016-30) Under the leadership of the Jedi, the Grand Army of the Republic forced the [Separatist Droid Army](/wiki/Separatist_Droid_Army "Separatist Droid Army") into full retreat and consequently won the [first battle](/wiki/First_Battle_of_Geonosis "First Battle of Geonosis") of the Clone Wars.[[2]](#cite_note-Episode_III-2) Clone production on Kamino continued during the war due to the Republic's need for more soldiers.[[32]](#cite_note-Queen's_Hope-32) In the wake of the Republic victory on Geonosis, [Count](/wiki/Count "Count") Dooku—the alter ego of Darth Tyranus—rallied a growing number of dissenting worlds to the Separatist cause, further dividing the Republic and forcing the clone troopers to fight the war on all fronts across the galaxy.[[33]](#cite_note-TCWFilm-33)

Throughout the conflict, clone troopers continuously demonstrated extreme loyalty to the Galactic Republic, especially their [Jedi Generals](/wiki/Jedi_General "Jedi General") and the Supreme Chancellor.[[1]](#cite_note-clonetroopers-1) The clones developed signs of individuality quickly, with the soldiers already showing themselves to be unique people during the first [weeks](/wiki/Standard_week "Standard week") of the conflict. Despite the Kaminoans claiming it would hamper their effectiveness, Jedi [General](/wiki/General "General") [Plo Koon](/wiki/Plo_Koon "Plo Koon") realized that the clones worked better as a unit when they were able to live out their individuality.[[32]](#cite_note-Queen's_Hope-32) Clones were expected by their brethren to be obedient to the chain of command, believing that their compliance reflected their commitment to the Republic. The [Advanced Recon Commando](/wiki/Advanced_Recon_Commando "Advanced Recon Commando") [Fives](/wiki/Fives "Fives") supported the system,[[34]](#cite_note-Dissent-34) and was driven by his sense of duty[[24]](#cite_note-TCW|Orders-24) as a loyal soldier of the Republic.[[35]](#cite_note-Carnage_of_Krell-35)

 [![Clone troopers served under the Knights of the Jedi Order, who held the rank of Jedi General in the Grand Army of the Republic.](data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIABAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAEALAAAAAABAAEAQAICTAEAOw%3D%3D)](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/0/0f/KiAdiMundiGeonosis-LaPR.png/revision/latest?cb=20120831044838) [![Clone troopers served under the Knights of the Jedi Order, who held the rank of Jedi General in the Grand Army of the Republic.](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/0/0f/KiAdiMundiGeonosis-LaPR.png/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/300?cb=20120831044838)](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/0/0f/KiAdiMundiGeonosis-LaPR.png/revision/latest?cb=20120831044838) 

Clone troopers served under the Knights of the Jedi Order, who held the rank of Jedi General in the Grand Army of the Republic.

 

Fives also believed that clone troopers were not disposable "numbers" and as such he opposed complying with orders that he considered to be wrong, although [Captain](/wiki/Captain "Captain") Rex maintained that a soldier should obey his [commanding officer](/wiki/Commanding_officer "Commanding officer") if he supported the system that they fought for.[[34]](#cite_note-Dissent-34) However, by the end of the bloody [Umbara Campaign](/wiki/Battle_of_Umbara "Battle of Umbara"), Rex agreed with Fives, feeling that clones sometimes needed to disobey their orders in order to do what was right.[[35]](#cite_note-Carnage_of_Krell-35) While the clones were conditioned to be absolutely obedient,[[4]](#cite_note-Episode_II-4) every clone developed his own unique identity. Insufficient or rushed field care led some clone veterans to have deep, physical scars. These soldiers wore their scars with pride, and some refused rehabilitative treatment to remove them.[[36]](#cite_note-Collapse-36)

The distinction between each clone ranged from loyal units,[[1]](#cite_note-clonetroopers-1) such as [Clone Commander](/wiki/Clone_Commander "Clone Commander") [Cody](/wiki/Cody "Cody")[[37]](#cite_note-Cody-37) and Captain Rex,[[27]](#cite_note-Rex-27) to a minority of clones who proved to be disloyal or uncommitted to the Republic's cause, such as [Sergeant](/wiki/Sergeant "Sergeant") Slick. Regarding service as [slavery](/wiki/Slavery "Slavery"), Slick betrayed the Republic by accepting bribes from the Separatists and was therefore arrested as a [traitor](/wiki/Treason "Treason") by the Grand Army.[[38]](#cite_note-Hidden_Enemy-38)

 [![The clones adopted nicknames and new hairstyles as they became more individualistic.](data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIABAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAEALAAAAAABAAEAQAICTAEAOw%3D%3D)](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/0/09/Clone_Commander_CotR.png/revision/latest?cb=20190717022749) [![The clones adopted nicknames and new hairstyles as they became more individualistic.](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/0/09/Clone_Commander_CotR.png/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/220?cb=20190717022749)](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/0/09/Clone_Commander_CotR.png/revision/latest?cb=20190717022749) 

The clones adopted nicknames and new hairstyles as they became more individualistic.

 

Another clone trooper displayed aberrant behavior by deserting the Grand Army and becoming a farmer under the name [Cut Lawquane](/wiki/Cut_Lawquane "Cut Lawquane"), joining a [family](/wiki/Lawquane_family "Lawquane family") on the planet [Saleucami](/wiki/Saleucami "Saleucami").[[39]](#cite_note-The_Deserter-39) Another clone deserter, [Muzzle](/wiki/Muzzle "Muzzle"), became head of the [Aurodium Sword](/wiki/Aurodium_Sword "Aurodium Sword") mercenary group. Through it, the clone continued to work with the Republic in a way, as the Aurodium Sword often took jobs as a security deal for Republic-aligned corporate personnel.[[36]](#cite_note-Collapse-36) Another clone deserted the military and took up a life that led them to a forest, where they wielded a [rifle](/wiki/Rifle "Rifle").[[40]](#cite_note-Clone_Deserter-40) For the most part, however, the clones found pride in their purpose as soldiers, and many continued to sacrifice their lives for the Republic as the war wore on.[[1]](#cite_note-clonetroopers-1)

Many of the clones that remained loyal throughout their service looked down on their brothers that had deserted, thinking them to be cowards or traitors. However, there were clones that were able to redeem themselves and willingly re-enter the ranks alongside their brothers. When a [squad](/wiki/Heater%27s_squad "Heater's squad") of deserters were given the opportunity to leave the army after completing [one last mission](/wiki/Assault_on_a_Separatist_weapons_depot "Assault on a Separatist weapons depot") together, the group came together and decided to remain in the army with their brothers.[[41]](#cite_note-Battle_Tales_4-41) Alternatively, Rex decided against bringing Lawquane back to the Republic when they met face-to-face during the [Battle of Saleucami](/wiki/Battle_of_Saleucami "Battle of Saleucami")[[39]](#cite_note-The_Deserter-39) in [21 BBY](/wiki/21_BBY "21 BBY").[[42]](#cite_note-21_BBY_Saleucami_Date-42) While he admitted it was supposed to be his duty to bring Lawquane in, he had fought beside the deserter and realized he was no coward, instead realizing that Lawquane was a man driven by a devotion to his family instead of the Republic.[[39]](#cite_note-The_Deserter-39) As such, Rex kept the secret of Lawquane's desertion to himself for the entire war.[[43]](#cite_note-Cut_and_Run-43)

 [![A sense of brotherhood existed among the clone troopers who had been bred to fight for the Galactic Republic.](data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIABAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAEALAAAAAABAAEAQAICTAEAOw%3D%3D)](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/9/93/Rex_inspirational.png/revision/latest?cb=20150608035048) [![A sense of brotherhood existed among the clone troopers who had been bred to fight for the Galactic Republic.](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/9/93/Rex_inspirational.png/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/250?cb=20150608035048)](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/9/93/Rex_inspirational.png/revision/latest?cb=20150608035048) 

A sense of brotherhood existed among the clone troopers who had been bred to fight for the Galactic Republic.

 

In addition to fighting alongside the Jedi and each other, the clone troopers viewed each other as brothers.[[38]](#cite_note-Hidden_Enemy-38) While admirable, this quality could keep them from seeing the bigger picture and make them willfully ignorant of the Republic's politics,[[36]](#cite_note-Collapse-36) but such a feeling also made the clones family to each other,[[38]](#cite_note-Hidden_Enemy-38)[[44]](#cite_note-Victory_and_Death-44) with troopers even using the word when talking to a fellow clone they had never met before.[[45]](#cite_note-Ahsoka-45) To show her that she belonged among them, the clones who served alongside a trans female clone gave her the name [Sister](/wiki/Sister "Sister").[[32]](#cite_note-Queen's_Hope-32) Troopers also tended to see their [barracks](/wiki/Barracks "Barracks") or [starships](/wiki/Starship "Starship") as places of work.[[15]](#cite_note-Rise-15) In addition, the clones viewed Kamino as their [homeworld](/wiki/Homeworld "Homeworld"). During the [Battle of Kamino](/wiki/Battle_of_Kamino "Battle of Kamino"), the clones fought bravely to prevent the Separatists from destroying the clone hatcheries as well as the remaining supply of their donor's genetic material. Their efforts resulted in a Republic victory, ensuring the continued production of clone troopers for the duration of the Clone Wars.[[8]](#cite_note-TSWB-8)

As the Clone Wars dragged on, the stress of combat and high casualties caused cracks and strains among the ranks of the clone soldiers. Personality quirks, once considered harmless or even essential to their mental development, began to express themselves in extreme and polarizing ways. Each unit created their own rituals, small ways to identify squad mates, those from the same [company](/wiki/Company "Company"), and veterans of specific campaigns. A soldier that talked about "cracking that crystal" identified themselves as a veteran of [Christophsis](/wiki/Christophsis "Christophsis") and the [assault](/wiki/Battle_of_Christophsis "Battle of Christophsis") on [Crystal City](/wiki/Chaleydonia "Chaleydonia"), while an officer calling targets "bugs" revealed he fought in the hives on Geonosis. While many clones respected a soldier with a different background, some felt separated by time, space, and the unique aspects of their struggle.[[36]](#cite_note-Collapse-36)

 [![Some clone troopers questioned their purpose and wondered what would become of them after the Clone Wars.](data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIABAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAEALAAAAAABAAEAQAICTAEAOw%3D%3D)](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/e/ef/501stLegion-Umbara.png/revision/latest?cb=20121126052245) [![Some clone troopers questioned their purpose and wondered what would become of them after the Clone Wars.](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/e/ef/501stLegion-Umbara.png/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/280?cb=20121126052245)](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/e/ef/501stLegion-Umbara.png/revision/latest?cb=20121126052245) 

Some clone troopers questioned their purpose and wondered what would become of them after the Clone Wars.

 

Though the vast majority of clones remained loyal to the Republic over the course of the three-year conflict, as time progressed a small number began to question their strict obedience. Naïve new clones found themselves fighting alongside veterans with years of combat experience that included the deaths of comrades, objectives gained and failed, and the often-ineffectual civilian Republic leadership. Consequently, some veterans developed a skepticism of Republic bureaucracy that shocked even the most cynical of rookie clones. Unlike most natural species where youth questioned their elders, it was the older clones of the Grand Army of the Republic who found themselves questioning their values and traditions. These clones still found comfort in the company of their brothers, but life no longer seemed as cut and dried to them.[[36]](#cite_note-Collapse-36)

Many clones realized that they were not held in high regard among the Republic and were treated as expendable soldiers who did not have personal feelings. This would help clones grow closer to each other and those who went against this convention, notably Jedi Generals Plo Koon[[46]](#cite_note-Rising_Malevolence-46) and [Obi-Wan Kenobi](/wiki/Obi-Wan_Kenobi "Obi-Wan Kenobi").[[47]](#cite_note-Battle_Tales_5-47) Although a divide of sorts existed between clones and Jedi, which was widened in the aftermath of General [Pong Krell](/wiki/Pong_Krell "Pong Krell")'s massacre of clone troopers during the [Umbara](/wiki/Umbara "Umbara") Campaign,[[48]](#cite_note-The_Dark_Side-48) clones remained very loyal to their leaders and generally considered them to be among their closest friends.[[24]](#cite_note-TCW|Orders-24) Indeed, the troops were known to form friendships with their Jedi officers,[[49]](#cite_note-K9-49) especially those that demonstrated loyalty back to them. Among the Jedi who were highly respected was [Padawan](/wiki/Padawan "Padawan") [Ahsoka Tano](/wiki/Ahsoka_Tano "Ahsoka Tano"),[[50]](#cite_note-Old_Friends-50) who believed all clones sounded different despite their genetic sameness; Yoda told her that was because she took the time needed to actually listen to them.[[45]](#cite_note-Ahsoka-45) Yoda also saw the clones as individuals, seeing that every trooper was different in the Force.[[51]](#cite_note-Ambush-51)

#### Public image[]

:   "*Valiant men, the clones have proven to be. Saved my life and yours they have many times. Believe in them we must.*"
:   ―Yoda[[13]](#cite_note-The_Lost_One-13)

 [![The Commission for the Protection of the Republic used clone troopers as wartime propaganda.](data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIABAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAEALAAAAAABAAEAQAICTAEAOw%3D%3D)](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/a/ae/Boys_in_white.jpg/revision/latest?cb=20170115165552) [![The Commission for the Protection of the Republic used clone troopers as wartime propaganda.](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/a/ae/Boys_in_white.jpg/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/200?cb=20170115165552)](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/a/ae/Boys_in_white.jpg/revision/latest?cb=20170115165552) 

The Commission for the Protection of the Republic used clone troopers as wartime propaganda.

 

Throughout the Clone Wars, clone troopers featured prominently in propaganda sponsored by both the Republic and Separatist media. The populist organization known as the [Commission for the Protection of the Republic](/wiki/Commission_for_the_Protection_of_the_Republic "Commission for the Protection of the Republic") (COMPOR) portrayed clones as the public face of the Republic's war effort, resulting in the publication of patriotic artwork such as *[Unite](/wiki/Unite "Unite")* and *[Support the Boys in White](/wiki/Support_the_Boys_in_White "Support the Boys in White")*. The posters expressed patriotism and civic duty to the citizens of the Republic. Part of a large outreach campaign, clone troopers became the symbol of the war effort, largely replacing the Jedi of previous years. Projecting strength and unity, they reminded citizens that their sacrifices were funding peace through military might.[[52]](#cite_note-Propaganda-52) Action figures of the clones were sold for children.[[53]](#cite_note-Axe_Forgets_trivia-53)

With there being significant debate amongst the public about the morality of sending living beings against an army of droids at the start of the war,[[32]](#cite_note-Queen's_Hope-32) COMPOR's messages were intended to ingrain the image of the clone trooper as brave soldiers risking all for freedom, democracy and the Republic.[[52]](#cite_note-Propaganda-52) Such was ironic given that the clones themselves enjoyed few individual liberties.[[54]](#cite_note-SWEasy-54) Although COMPOR also wanted to use the Jedi Order as a tool for propaganda, Chancellor Palpatine advised against this course of action, citing sympathy for the Jedi's reluctant acceptance of their new role during wartime. As a result, very few [examples](/wiki/Jedi_Unite_for_Peace "Jedi Unite for Peace") of pro-Jedi messages exist as COMPOR devoted their full attention to promoting support for the clone troopers as well as loyalty to the Republic and, in particular, Chancellor Palpatine.[[52]](#cite_note-Propaganda-52)

 [![Civilians protested Jedi and clones alike, believing both groups were responsible for prolonging the conflict.](data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIABAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAEALAAAAAABAAEAQAICTAEAOw%3D%3D)](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/c/c1/Anti-Jedi_protest_signs.jpg/revision/latest?cb=20130212161217) [![Civilians protested Jedi and clones alike, believing both groups were responsible for prolonging the conflict.](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/c/c1/Anti-Jedi_protest_signs.jpg/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/250?cb=20130212161217)](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/c/c1/Anti-Jedi_protest_signs.jpg/revision/latest?cb=20130212161217) 

Civilians protested Jedi and clones alike, believing both groups were responsible for prolonging the conflict.

 

By contrast, the Confederacy of Independent Systems decried the clone army as a biological abomination—an inhumane practice in which weaponized embryos were carried to artificial term and turned into disposable killing machines. The Separatist cause was, therefore, portrayed as the more "humane" approach due to the Confederacy's use of battle droids.[[52]](#cite_note-Propaganda-52) In some way, this dehumanizing sentiment was shared in the Republic. Under Republic law, clone troopers were property of the Galactic Republic. However, Nala Se took the position that the clones were Kaminoan property, as they had been created in the laboratories of Kamino.[[22]](#cite_note-TCW|Fugitive-22) Senator [Christo](/wiki/Christo "Christo") of the Galactic Senate considered the clones disposable, supported increasing the cloning production, and rationalized their deaths as the fulfillment of their purpose.[[55]](#cite_note-Pursuit-55) An [anti-clone sentiment](/wiki/Anti-clone_sentiment "Anti-clone sentiment") persisted after the war's end and into the [Imperial Era](/wiki/Imperial_Era "Imperial Era").[[56]](#cite_note-The_Summit-56)

Galactic citizens could also be unaware of the friendships that could grow between clones and Jedi; [farmer](/wiki/Farmer "Farmer") [Kaeden Larte](/wiki/Kaeden_Larte "Kaeden Larte") believed clones only followed Jedi like Ahsoka Tano because they were superior officers, unaware of how[[45]](#cite_note-Ahsoka-45) Jedi like Tano had truly earned the troopers' respect.[[50]](#cite_note-Old_Friends-50) As the war carried on, more Republic citizens became disillusioned with the seemingly endless conflict, allowing Separatist and antiwar propaganda to take root in the Republic's territory. Widespread discontent began to erode the clones' public image despite COMPOR's efforts; even their civilian-coined nickname "Boys in White" backfired as antiwar activists pointed to the fact that the clones were barely thirteen years old by the third year of the Clone Wars.[[52]](#cite_note-Propaganda-52)

### Order 66[]

#### Sith conspiracy[]

:   "*I like a good mystery.*"  
    "*Yeah? You ever hear the one about the people engineered to kill, engineered to kill their best friends, their leaders, and they don't even know it?*"
:   ―[Jay Igno](/wiki/Jay_Igno "Jay Igno") and Fives[[24]](#cite_note-TCW|Orders-24)

 [![The Sith conspiracy against the Jedi was jeopardized by a defective clone that prematurely executed Order 66.](data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIABAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAEALAAAAAABAAEAQAICTAEAOw%3D%3D)](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/3/3b/PrematureExecution-TU.png/revision/latest?cb=20150408070427) [![The Sith conspiracy against the Jedi was jeopardized by a defective clone that prematurely executed Order 66.](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/3/3b/PrematureExecution-TU.png/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/250?cb=20150408070427)](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/3/3b/PrematureExecution-TU.png/revision/latest?cb=20150408070427) 

The Sith conspiracy against the Jedi was jeopardized by a defective clone that prematurely executed Order 66.

 

Near the end of the war, Order 66 was nearly discovered by the Jedi. Tup was a clone trooper in the 501st [Legion](/wiki/Legion "Legion") who became mentally unstable when his inhibitor chip malfunctioned during the [Battle of Ringo Vinda](/wiki/Battle_of_Ringo_Vinda "Battle of Ringo Vinda"), causing him to betray and kill Jedi [General](/wiki/General "General") [Tiplar](/wiki/Tiplar "Tiplar").[[57]](#cite_note-The_Unknown-57) This premature execution of Order 66 resulted in an investigation by the Republic, the Jedi, and the Kaminoans. The Sith also took an interest in the matter; Count Dooku—whom Lama Su and Nala Se knew only as "Tyranus," their secret benefactor—instructed the Kaminoans to prevent the Jedi from discovering the true purpose of the inhibitor chips.[[20]](#cite_note-TCW|Conspiracy-20) Tyranus was also disturbed by the degree of individuality that the clones displayed in spite of their psychological conditioning; Nala Se believed that the Jedi were responsible for encouraging greater creative thinking in the clones. Nevertheless, she was certain that, with the exception of Tup's damaged chip, the rest of the chips would function according to their design.[[22]](#cite_note-TCW|Fugitive-22)

 [![The Coruscant Guard was deployed to hunt Fives, a clone framed for treason.](data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIABAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAEALAAAAAABAAEAQAICTAEAOw%3D%3D)](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/1/16/CoruscantGuardssearching.png/revision/latest?cb=20200606004751) [![The Coruscant Guard was deployed to hunt Fives, a clone framed for treason.](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/1/16/CoruscantGuardssearching.png/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/250?cb=20200606004751)](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/1/16/CoruscantGuardssearching.png/revision/latest?cb=20200606004751) 

The Coruscant Guard was deployed to hunt Fives, a clone framed for treason.

 

During the investigation, the ARC trooper Fives became increasingly convinced that the inhibitor chip was part of a conspiracy against the Republic and the Jedi.[[20]](#cite_note-TCW|Conspiracy-20)[[22]](#cite_note-TCW|Fugitive-22) Against Nala Se's advice, he was allowed to plead his case to Chancellor Palpatine. However, their meeting led the ARC trooper to believe that the Chancellor was involved in the conspiracy, although he was unaware of to what extent. Jedi Master [Shaak Ti](/wiki/Shaak_Ti "Shaak Ti") witnessed Fives' attempt to assassinate the Chancellor and prevented him from succeeding. Although Fives [escaped](/wiki/Escape_from_the_Grand_Republic_Medical_Facility "Escape from the Grand Republic Medical Facility") from the [Grand Republic Medical Facility](/wiki/Grand_Republic_Medical_Facility "Grand Republic Medical Facility"), he was confronted by a group of Coruscant shock troopers led by Clone [Commander](/wiki/Commander "Commander") [Fox](/wiki/Fox "Fox") while attempting to warn Jedi General [Anakin Skywalker](/wiki/Anakin_Skywalker "Anakin Skywalker") and Captain Rex. After Fives was killed by Fox, Palpatine convinced the Jedi that a rare parasite from [Ringo Vinda](/wiki/Ringo_Vinda "Ringo Vinda") was responsible for the malfunction in Tup and Fives, and that the clone troopers had to be inoculated to prevent their inhibitor chips from malfunctioning.[[24]](#cite_note-TCW|Orders-24)

Shortly before dying, Tup and Fives—both of whom had their chips removed—described Order 66 as a mission that they repeatedly experienced in their nightmares.[[20]](#cite_note-TCW|Conspiracy-20)[[24]](#cite_note-TCW|Orders-24) With their deaths and the removal of any evidence that could alert the Jedi to the existence of Order 66, the Chancellor convinced the Jedi Council that the clone troopers did require their inhibitor chips. Still, Rex, who had held Fives as he died,[[24]](#cite_note-TCW|Orders-24) submitted a grievance report, where he stated the inhibitor chips could have an alternate purpose. While he was not sure if he believed it and knew the report would be ignored, Rex believed he owed it to Fives to record what he had learned.[[9]](#cite_note-Shattered-9)

 [![Fives was killed before he could expose the plot to turn the clone troopers against their Jedi Generals.](data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIABAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAEALAAAAAABAAEAQAICTAEAOw%3D%3D)](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/e/ef/GoodbyeFives-O.png/revision/latest?cb=20140726105615) [![Fives was killed before he could expose the plot to turn the clone troopers against their Jedi Generals.](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/e/ef/GoodbyeFives-O.png/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/250?cb=20140726105615)](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/e/ef/GoodbyeFives-O.png/revision/latest?cb=20140726105615) 

Fives was killed before he could expose the plot to turn the clone troopers against their Jedi Generals.

 

The death of Fives did not completely ensure the secrecy of Order 66, however. The Jedi Council began inquiring into the specific circumstances regarding the mysterious death of Sifo-Dyas, the founder of the clone army. Alarmed by the Jedi's interest in the matter, Darth Sidious tasked his apprentice with the responsibility of eliminating any remaining loose ends that could connect the Sith with the creation of the clones. Darth Tyranus journeyed to the planet [Oba Diah](/wiki/Oba_Diah "Oba Diah") and killed [Minister](/wiki/Minister "Minister") [Lom Pyke](/wiki/Lom_Pyke "Lom Pyke") of the [Pyke](/wiki/Pyke "Pyke") Syndicate, but not before the Pyke revealed to the Jedi that Tyranus and Dooku were one and the same.[[13]](#cite_note-The_Lost_One-13)

The Jedi Council was disturbed by the revelation of the Sith Order's involvement in the creation of the clones. Yet in spite of their suspicions regarding the reasons the Sith would provide the Jedi with an army, the Council ultimately chose to conceal their findings from the public and the government, fearing that such a discovery would undermine public confidence in the war. Grand Master Yoda insisted that their priority remained the same, to end the war as swiftly as possible before the Sith's plans came to fruition. Moreover, the Grand Master believed that the clones were genuinely loyal to their Jedi leaders, having saved them on numerous occasions throughout the war.[[13]](#cite_note-The_Lost_One-13)

#### Fall of the Jedi[]

:   "*How widespread is this?*"  
    "*Ahsoka, it's all of us. The entire Grand Army of the Republic has been ordered to hunt down and destroy the Jedi Knights.*"
:   ―Ahsoka Tano and Rex, on Order 66 — ![20?cb=20250116042720](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/e/ee/Quote-audio.png/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/20?cb=20250116042720) [Link](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/1/11/HowWidespread-Shattered.flac/revision/latest?cb=20250327205815)▶️ ([file info](/wiki/File:HowWidespread-Shattered.flac "File:HowWidespread-Shattered.flac"))[[9]](#cite_note-Shattered-9)

 [![Utapau was invaded by the Republic clone army, their objective to destroy General Grievous and end the Clone Wars.](data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIABAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAEALAAAAAABAAEAQAICTAEAOw%3D%3D)](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/8/8d/212th_Battalion.png/revision/latest?cb=20151030113059) [![Utapau was invaded by the Republic clone army, their objective to destroy General Grievous and end the Clone Wars.](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/8/8d/212th_Battalion.png/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/250?cb=20151030113059)](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/8/8d/212th_Battalion.png/revision/latest?cb=20151030113059) 

Utapau was invaded by the Republic clone army, their objective to destroy General Grievous and end the Clone Wars.

 

After three years of constant warfare,[[1]](#cite_note-clonetroopers-1) the Separatist forces [attacked](/wiki/Battle_of_Coruscant "Battle of Coruscant")[[2]](#cite_note-Episode_III-2) the Republic [capital](/wiki/Capital "Capital") world[[58]](#cite_note-coruscant-58) of Coruscant and managed to abduct Chancellor Palpatine in the process, a plan which was organized by Sidious in order to bring Anakin to the dark side and make him his apprentice.[[1]](#cite_note-clonetroopers-1) By the time of the battle, a full third of the original deployment of clones had been killed in action. Those who survived wore armor that had been dirtied and dented by conflict.[[59]](#cite_note-SWCEUAE-59) The clone troopers rallied to Coruscant's defense while the Jedi Knights Obi-Wan Kenobi and Anakin Skywalker rescued the Chancellor. During the battle, Darth Tyranus was betrayed by Sidious, who swayed Skywalker to killing him. With Dooku dead, this brought the Clone Wars closer to a successful conclusion for the Republic. The Jedi Council moved to capitalize on the momentum gained by Tyranus' death in the hope of ending the war.[[2]](#cite_note-Episode_III-2)

The Grand Army continued to fight the war on various worlds across the galaxy, including [Mygeeto](/wiki/Mygeeto "Mygeeto"), [Felucia](/wiki/Felucia "Felucia"), [Cato Neimoidia](/wiki/Cato_Neimoidia "Cato Neimoidia"), and [Saleucami](/wiki/Saleucami "Saleucami"). New fronts were opened as clone troopers were deployed to [Kashyyyk](/wiki/Kashyyyk "Kashyyyk") and [Utapau](/wiki/Utapau "Utapau"); and other planets as part of the [Outer Rim Sieges](/wiki/Outer_Rim_Sieges "Outer Rim Sieges"). [Gree](/wiki/Gree_(clone_trooper) "Gree (clone trooper)") and the [41st Elite Corps](/wiki/41st_Elite_Corps "41st Elite Corps") fought side-by-side with the [Wookiees](/wiki/Wookiee "Wookiee") in the [Battle of Kashyyyk](/wiki/Battle_of_Kashyyyk "Battle of Kashyyyk"), under the command of Yoda, while Kenobi and Cody oversaw the [Battle of Utapau](/wiki/Battle_of_Utapau "Battle of Utapau") between the [212th Attack Battalion](/wiki/212th_Attack_Battalion "212th Attack Battalion") and General [Grievous](/wiki/Grievous "Grievous")'s [droid](/wiki/Droid "Droid") army.[[2]](#cite_note-Episode_III-2) By this time, the [332nd Division](/wiki/332nd_Division "332nd Division") had been formed out of Skywalker's 501st Legion in order to participate in the [Siege of Mandalore](/wiki/Siege_of_Mandalore "Siege of Mandalore"). The new division was placed under the command of Rex, who was promoted to the rank of Clone Commander, while Skywalker's former Padawan, the [Force-Sensitive Outcast](/wiki/Force-Sensitive_Outcast "Force-Sensitive Outcast") Tano, accompanied the 332nd as an [advisor](/wiki/Advisor "Advisor").[[50]](#cite_note-Old_Friends-50)

 [![Darth Sidious contacted Clone Commander Cody, as well as other clone officers, and instructed them to execute Order 66.](data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIABAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAEALAAAAAABAAEAQAICTAEAOw%3D%3D)](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/1/18/Execute_Order_66.png/revision/latest?cb=20121210185439) [![Darth Sidious contacted Clone Commander Cody, as well as other clone officers, and instructed them to execute Order 66.](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/1/18/Execute_Order_66.png/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/250?cb=20121210185439)](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/1/18/Execute_Order_66.png/revision/latest?cb=20121210185439) 

Darth Sidious contacted Clone Commander Cody, as well as other clone officers, and instructed them to execute Order 66.

 

As the Republic drew closer to achieving total victory in the Clone Wars, Chancellor Palpatine revealed his deception and true identity as Darth Sidious to the Jedi, provoking an immediate response from the Jedi Council. The consequent [confrontation](/wiki/Duel_in_Palpatine%27s_office "Duel in Palpatine's office") between the Council and the Dark [Lord](/wiki/Lord "Lord") ended in the deaths of several Jedi Masters, including Mace Windu, and Skywalker's fall to the [dark side of the Force](/wiki/Dark_side_of_the_Force "Dark side of the Force"). Now anointed as the Sith Lord Darth Vader, Sidious' new apprentice participated in the 501st Legion's [assault](/wiki/Operation:_Knightfall "Operation: Knightfall") on the [Jedi Temple](/wiki/Imperial_Palace "Imperial Palace"). Under the influence of Order 66, the 501st clone troopers stormed the Temple and exterminated the Jedi within. None of the Jedi were spared, including the [younglings](/wiki/Youngling "Youngling").[[2]](#cite_note-Episode_III-2) Some clone troopers then donned Jedi robes as [disguised Jedi](/wiki/Disguised_Clone_Trooper "Disguised Clone Trooper") to entrap any Jedi who tried to enter the building.[[60]](#cite_note-ROTSFrench_Novel-60)

Around the same time, Darth Sidious issued Order 66 to the clone troopers throughout the galaxy—declaring every Jedi an enemy of the Republic. Order 66 triggered the hidden chips within the clones,[[1]](#cite_note-clonetroopers-1) erasing their loyalty to the Jedi[[19]](#cite_note-Aftermath_(episode)-19) and brainwashing them[[23]](#cite_note-Journeys:_Beginnings-23) into believing that the Jedi were traitors to the Republic who deserved execution.[[19]](#cite_note-Aftermath_(episode)-19) Losing their freewill and identities with the mere activation of a chip through a voice command,[[45]](#cite_note-Ahsoka-45) the overwhelming majority of the clones suddenly turned on their unsuspecting allies; caught off guard by their own troops betraying them, the Jedi across numerous worlds were largely slaughtered by their clone troopers. However, there were a handful of clones that resisted the command by removing their biochips. The members of Clone Force 99, excluding Crosshair, did not obey the command as well, as their genetic enhancements made them immune to their chips.[[19]](#cite_note-Aftermath_(episode)-19) With the exception of a few survivors, the Jedi were all but extinct in the aftermath of the initial execution of Order 66.[[2]](#cite_note-Episode_III-2) In addition, this protocol did not end with members of the Jedi Order, as clone troopers who failed to comply with the order were to be killed as well.[[9]](#cite_note-Shattered-9)

 [![Across the galaxy, the clone troopers turned against their Jedi leaders as a result of their programmed compliance with Order 66.](data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIABAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAEALAAAAAABAAEAQAICTAEAOw%3D%3D)](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/7/77/Order66Ahsoka-Shattered.png/revision/latest?cb=20200502213624) [![Across the galaxy, the clone troopers turned against their Jedi leaders as a result of their programmed compliance with Order 66.](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/7/77/Order66Ahsoka-Shattered.png/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/250?cb=20200502213624)](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/7/77/Order66Ahsoka-Shattered.png/revision/latest?cb=20200502213624) 

Across the galaxy, the clone troopers turned against their Jedi leaders as a result of their programmed compliance with Order 66.

 

Aboard the [*Venator*-class Star Destroyer](/wiki/Venator-class_Star_Destroyer "Venator-class Star Destroyer") *[Tribunal](/wiki/Tribunal "Tribunal")*,[[61]](#cite_note-Join_the_Battle-61) Tano and the rogue Sith Lord Darth [Maul](/wiki/Maul "Maul") were [also targeted](/wiki/Skirmish_aboard_the_Tribunal "Skirmish aboard the Tribunal") by the clones of the 332nd Division shortly after their victory on [Mandalore](/wiki/Mandalore "Mandalore"). Commander Rex managed to resist his chip's control for long enough to tell Tano to find Fives. When Rex finally fell victim to its control, Tano escaped the troopers and released Maul from [captivity](/wiki/Mandalorian_vault "Mandalorian vault"), intending to have him be a distraction. Tano then looked into Fives, finding Rex's grievance report on the chips. With the help of astromech droids [R7-A7](/wiki/R7-A7 "R7-A7"), [CH-33P](/wiki/CH-33P "CH-33P"), and [RG-G1](/wiki/RG-G1 "RG-G1"), Tano incapacitated Rex in order to remove his chip, which restored his loyalty to Ahsoka.[[9]](#cite_note-Shattered-9)

Freed from the influence of the control chip, Rex informed Tano that the entire Grand Army had turned against the Jedi.[[9]](#cite_note-Shattered-9) The former Jedi, the Clone Commander, and the astromech droids planned to steal a [shuttle](/wiki/Shuttle "Shuttle") from the Venator's main hangar; Rex complied with Tano's wishes to only stun the clones in their path, despite knowing that his brethren fully intended to execute them as traitors to the state. Elsewhere, Maul continued to move through the [warship](/wiki/Warship "Warship"), ultimately entering and destroying the [hyperdrive](/wiki/Hyperdrive "Hyperdrive") room. This pulled the [Star Destroyer](/wiki/Star_Destroyer "Star Destroyer") out of [hyperspace](/wiki/Hyperspace "Hyperspace") and into the gravitational field of a [moon](/wiki/Unidentified_moon "Unidentified moon"), but the 332nd remained determined to kill Tano, even if it would result in their own deaths. Even though the clone troopers blocked their path to a [*Nu*-class attack/transport shuttle](/wiki/Nu-class_attack/transport_shuttle "Nu-class attack/transport shuttle"), Tano did not want to harm the soldiers, but Rex, who shed a tear, informed her that the clones were willing to die executing Order 66.[[44]](#cite_note-Victory_and_Death-44)

Tano was still unwilling to take their lives and devised a plan to stall the troops; while R7 prepared to drop parts of the floor, Rex distracted [Clone Lieutenant](/wiki/Clone_Lieutenant "Clone Lieutenant") [Jesse](/wiki/Jesse "Jesse"), and the other clones by bringing Tano at gunpoint before them. He argued that while Order 66 called for the execution of all Jedi, Tano had not been a Jedi for some time. Jesse was not dissuaded from his task, however, stating to Rex that they were under direct orders from Darth Sidious to kill the former Jedi as well as any clone who refused to comply with their protocol. When Rex made a final plea to Jesse, the ARC trooper accused his former friend as a traitor to the Republic, and subsequently demoted him in rank from Commander, and sentenced him to die alongside Tano via firing squad in accordance with Order 66.[[44]](#cite_note-Victory_and_Death-44)

 [![Ahsoka Tano buried her clone troopers before hiding from the newly risen Galactic Empire.](data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIABAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAEALAAAAAABAAEAQAICTAEAOw%3D%3D)](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/9/9c/AhsokaGraveyard-VaD.png/revision/latest?cb=20200504142158) [![Ahsoka Tano buried her clone troopers before hiding from the newly risen Galactic Empire.](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/9/9c/AhsokaGraveyard-VaD.png/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/250?cb=20200504142158)](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/9/9c/AhsokaGraveyard-VaD.png/revision/latest?cb=20200504142158) 

Ahsoka Tano buried her clone troopers before hiding from the newly risen Galactic Empire.

 

The clone troopers destroyed the astromechs in the ensuing firefight, which Maul used as a distraction to escape from the doomed Star Destroyer. Jesse and the remaining clones were killed when their warship crashed into the moon, while Tano and Rex escaped using a [BTL-B Y-wing starfighter/bomber](/wiki/BTL-B_Y-wing_starfighter/bomber "BTL-B Y-wing starfighter/bomber") before the *Tribunal* entered the [atmosphere](/wiki/Atmosphere "Atmosphere"). They recovered the clones' bodies and buried them at the crash site, using their helmets to mark each clone's grave. Tano then abandoned her[[44]](#cite_note-Victory_and_Death-44) [lightsabers](/wiki/Ahsoka_Tano%27s_lightsabers "Ahsoka Tano's lightsabers")[[62]](#cite_note-DB:Ahsoka-62) at the gravesite[[44]](#cite_note-Victory_and_Death-44) and eventually parted ways with Rex, both agreeing to leave for the [Outer Rim Territories](/wiki/Outer_Rim_Territories "Outer Rim Territories").[[45]](#cite_note-Ahsoka-45)

### The first stormtroopers[]

:   [![icon](data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIABAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAEALAAAAAABAAEAQAICTAEAOw%3D%3D)](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/0/04/Blue_Glass_Arrow.svg/revision/latest?cb=20090726033133) Main article: [Stormtrooper](/wiki/Stormtrooper "Stormtrooper")

#### The future of clone trooper program[]

:   "*I heard they shut down the facilities on Kamino. They'll train up the last batch of clones and that's it.*"  
    "*But that's crazy. Who will protect the Empire?*"  
    "*Don't know, Kicker. But it won't be* us*. We get to pack up old Jedi way stations and crate everything back to Coruscant. I think our fighting days are* done*.*"
:   ―Ding and Kicker discuss rumors[[3]](#cite_note-Dark_Lord_2-3)

 [![The first generation of Imperial stormtroopers consisted of the clones that once served the Galactic Republic.](data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIABAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAEALAAAAAABAAEAQAICTAEAOw%3D%3D)](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/c/cd/Darth_Vader_Dark_Lord_of_the_Sith_2_Mundo_textless.png/revision/latest?cb=20180429032514) [![The first generation of Imperial stormtroopers consisted of the clones that once served the Galactic Republic.](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/c/cd/Darth_Vader_Dark_Lord_of_the_Sith_2_Mundo_textless.png/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/200?cb=20180429032514)](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/c/cd/Darth_Vader_Dark_Lord_of_the_Sith_2_Mundo_textless.png/revision/latest?cb=20180429032514) 

The first generation of Imperial stormtroopers consisted of the clones that once served the Galactic Republic.

 

The destruction of the Jedi Order allowed the Sith to reclaim [control](/wiki/Fascism "Fascism") of the galaxy through Sidious,[[2]](#cite_note-Episode_III-2) having used the clone troopers as their secret weapon.[[1]](#cite_note-clonetroopers-1) With the government and the military under his control, Sidious [reorganized](/wiki/Proclamation_of_the_New_Order "Proclamation of the New Order") the Republic into the [First Galactic Empire](/wiki/Galactic_Empire "Galactic Empire") and assumed the mantle of [Galactic Emperor](/wiki/Galactic_Emperor "Galactic Emperor").[[2]](#cite_note-Episode_III-2) This was followed by sweeping alterations that distinguished the [New Order](/wiki/New_Order "New Order") from the old system.[[63]](#cite_note-EotG-63) When the conflict ended,[[64]](#cite_note-Expert_Guide-64) the clone troopers who survived the Clone Wars went on to serve the Empire[[8]](#cite_note-TSWB-8) as the first generation of Imperial [stormtroopers](/wiki/Stormtrooper "Stormtrooper")[[7]](#cite_note-stormtroopers-7) on the decree of the Emperor.[[65]](#cite_note-DS_Incredibuilds-65) They formed the backbone of the [Imperial Army](/wiki/Imperial_Army "Imperial Army")[[8]](#cite_note-TSWB-8) during the early years of the [Imperial Era](/wiki/Imperial_Era "Imperial Era").[[66]](#cite_note-AND-66)

As elite shock troops, clones were responsible for projecting the [Emperor](/wiki/Emperor "Emperor")'s will over the galaxy and destroying threats to his reign.[[7]](#cite_note-stormtroopers-7) Without the Jedi[[67]](#cite_note-Aftermath_Episode_Guide-67) who encouraged their soldiers to think as individuals instead of only adhering to protocol,[[68]](#cite_note-Clone_Armor_DB-68) the clone troopers became fully obedient[[67]](#cite_note-Aftermath_Episode_Guide-67) as a result of the programming enforced by their control chips.[[19]](#cite_note-Aftermath_(episode)-19) Changing their armor[[69]](#cite_note-Best_of_the_Batch-69) to its basic, blank white state,[[67]](#cite_note-Aftermath_Episode_Guide-67) the clones became cold and unfriendly,[[69]](#cite_note-Best_of_the_Batch-69) focusing solely on their protocol and orders. While the clones retained a degree of individuality, such as a sense of humor, when off-duty, the troopers by and large[[19]](#cite_note-Aftermath_(episode)-19) adopted uniformity, which was symbolized by the sudden lack of personalization amongst their armor,[[69]](#cite_note-Best_of_the_Batch-69) and were forced to despise their former Jedi friends.[[70]](#cite_note-TLP_5-70)

 [![Under orders from Imperial Intelligence, clone troopers would arrest dozens of Senators on charges of conspiring with the Jedi's rebellion.](data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIABAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAEALAAAAAABAAEAQAICTAEAOw%3D%3D)](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/9/94/TRF_Senatorial_arrests_fixed.png/revision/latest?cb=20250226055957) [![Under orders from Imperial Intelligence, clone troopers would arrest dozens of Senators on charges of conspiring with the Jedi's rebellion.](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/9/94/TRF_Senatorial_arrests_fixed.png/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/200?cb=20250226055957)](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/9/94/TRF_Senatorial_arrests_fixed.png/revision/latest?cb=20250226055957) 

Under orders from Imperial Intelligence, clone troopers would arrest dozens of Senators on charges of conspiring with the Jedi's rebellion.

 

Under Imperial orders, clones carried out the [Senatorial arrests](/wiki/Senatorial_arrests "Senatorial arrests")[[71]](#cite_note-Rebel_Files-71) and were deployed to clear out former Jedi bases.[[3]](#cite_note-Dark_Lord_2-3) They also enforced order by arresting civilians for actions as small as engaging in fights, which confused the [smuggler](/wiki/Smuggler "Smuggler") [Has Obitt](/wiki/Has_Obitt "Has Obitt"); according to Obitt, during the war the clones would have been the people that started a bar fight, yet the troops were now breaking them up.[[72]](#cite_note-Catalyst-72) Despite the their role in the formation and enforcement of the early Empire,[[3]](#cite_note-Dark_Lord_2-3) the value of all clone troopers was called into question by officials like [Governor](/wiki/Governor "Governor") [Wilhuff Tarkin](/wiki/Wilhuff_Tarkin "Wilhuff Tarkin")[[19]](#cite_note-Aftermath_(episode)-19) and [Vice Admiral](/wiki/Vice_Admiral "Vice Admiral") [Edmon Rampart](/wiki/Edmon_Rampart "Edmon Rampart"), [Imperial officers](/wiki/Imperial_officer "Imperial officer") who believed that a service conscription and recruitment force was more affordable and reliable than the cloning operation on Kamino.[[21]](#cite_note-Replacements-21)

Furthermore, the clones were originally bred to be soldiers of the Republic and not the Empire:[[73]](#cite_note-War-Mantle-73) to a number of high ranking Imperials, clone troopers remained a reminder of the past and, like that past, needed to be swept away.[[74]](#cite_note-BB_S2-74) While the activation of their control chips held the clones loyalty firmly in place to the new regime,[[19]](#cite_note-Aftermath_(episode)-19) the founders of War-Mantle knew recruited soldiers would be able to swear loyalty to the new Empire alone[[73]](#cite_note-War-Mantle-73) and do so of their own free will.[[21]](#cite_note-Replacements-21) Tarkin also disliked the level of individuality the clones had come to develop under the leadership of the Jedi.[[56]](#cite_note-The_Summit-56) Tarkin visited Kamino in the aftermath of Order 66 to inspect the clones and determine whether the Empire had any further use of them.[[19]](#cite_note-Aftermath_(episode)-19)

 [![Admiral and Governor Wilhuff Tarkin informed the Kaminoans of the Empire's plans to replace clones with conscripts.](data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIABAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAEALAAAAAABAAEAQAICTAEAOw%3D%3D)](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/a/a3/Tarkin-arrives-on-Kamino.png/revision/latest?cb=20220101192826) [![Admiral and Governor Wilhuff Tarkin informed the Kaminoans of the Empire's plans to replace clones with conscripts.](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/a/a3/Tarkin-arrives-on-Kamino.png/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/250?cb=20220101192826)](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/a/a3/Tarkin-arrives-on-Kamino.png/revision/latest?cb=20220101192826) 

Admiral and Governor Wilhuff Tarkin informed the Kaminoans of the Empire's plans to replace clones with conscripts.

 

Prime Minister Lama Su was surprised to learn the purpose of the admiral's visit, having long counted on the support of Chancellor Palpatine in the past. Tarkin informed the Kaminoan politician that Palpatine's priorities had changed following the end of the Clone Wars and his ascension as the Emperor. Lama Su opposed the shutdown of the cloning facilities, citing the Kaminoans' contracts which stipulated the continued production of clone troopers. The Admiral countered that this agreement had been made between Kamino and the Empire's predecessor, the Republic, which no longer existed. While he agreed with the Prime Minister's point that the newly risen Empire needed more soldiers to maintain order in the galaxy, Tarkin believed that this objective could be achieved through a service conscription force.[[19]](#cite_note-Aftermath_(episode)-19)

The Prime Minister dismissed the notion of replacing clone soldiers with recruits which he regarded as inherently inferior to his creations, but Tarkin was concerned that the clone trooper program was too expensive to maintain. He therefore considered conscription and recruitment a cost effective solution to the Empire's need for increased manpower.[[19]](#cite_note-Aftermath_(episode)-19) Although cloning operations would continue for a short while longer,[[21]](#cite_note-Replacements-21) rumors spread across the clone ranks during the early Imperial Era that the Empire had already halted the Kamino operations, making clones such as [Ding](/wiki/Ding "Ding") and [Kicker](/wiki/Kicker "Kicker") ponder the Empire's future and the fate of their kind. Knowing that the clone army had only one generation left in its future, older clones dreaded the notion of retirement and, therefore, sought ways to remain on active duty, such as joining the [Emperor's Royal Guard](/wiki/Emperor%27s_Royal_Guard "Emperor's Royal Guard").[[3]](#cite_note-Dark_Lord_2-3)

 [![Darth Vader wiped out a unit of clone troopers who mistook him for a Jedi.](data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIABAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAEALAAAAAABAAEAQAICTAEAOw%3D%3D)](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/3/32/ShouldNotHaveSaidThat-2017DarthVader2.png/revision/latest?cb=20230314201209) [![Darth Vader wiped out a unit of clone troopers who mistook him for a Jedi.](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/3/32/ShouldNotHaveSaidThat-2017DarthVader2.png/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/300?cb=20230314201209)](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/3/32/ShouldNotHaveSaidThat-2017DarthVader2.png/revision/latest?cb=20230314201209) 

Darth Vader wiped out a unit of clone troopers who mistook him for a Jedi.

 

With clones beginning to be dispatched to secure Jedi sites instead of active combat, Ding and Kicker were part of the clone force sent to a [Mid Rim](/wiki/Mid_Rim_Territories "Mid Rim Territories") [way station](/wiki/Space_station "Space station") named the *[Brighthome](/wiki/Brighthome "Brighthome")*, which the former trooper feared represented the overall future of their kind; while new soldiers would be able to fight the enemies of the Empire, he feared the clones would be reduced to clean up operations. Nevertheless, the two thought they had a chance to prove themselves when an individual believed to be a surviving Jedi [attacked the station](/wiki/Attack_on_Brighthome "Attack on Brighthome"). In reality, the intruder was Darth Vader, who had elected to not send out his clearance codes to fight the clones aboard. Vader slaughtered the majority of the troops who came against him, and, although Ding and Kicker briefly gained an advantage over the Sith Lord, Vader killed both with a [Force choke](/wiki/Force_choke "Force choke"), allowing him to leave for the moon of [Al'doleem](/wiki/Al%27doleem "Al'doleem").[[3]](#cite_note-Dark_Lord_2-3)

With the exception of Crosshair, the defective clones of Clone Force 99, meanwhile, remained largely unaffected by their inhibitor biochips. Sent back to Kamino to listen to Palpatine's proclamation of the Empire, they also met the young female clone Omega, who was still kept on Kamino[[19]](#cite_note-Aftermath_(episode)-19) should the Kaminoans need a backup of Jango Fett's genetic information.[[18]](#cite_note-Bounty_Lost-18) While Tarkin was interested in welcoming Clone Force 99 into the Imperial Army for their skills, he was concerned by their individuality and willingness to go against orders. Dispatching on a [mission](/wiki/Mission_to_Onderon_(Clone_Force_99) "Mission to Onderon (Clone Force 99)") to wipe out supposed Separatist insurgents as a test, Clone Force 99 instead encountered civilians being protected by former Republic fighter [Saw Gerrera](/wiki/Saw_Gerrera "Saw Gerrera"), convincing most of the squad to abandon the Empire. With the squad returning to Kamino to rescue Omega, Crosshair was welcomed into the Empire after his chip was amplified. Crosshair led the effort to kill his former squadmates as they [escaped](/wiki/Escape_from_Kamino "Escape from Kamino"), failing when Se secretly overrode the hangar door controls to give Omega a chance to escape with Clone Force 99.[[19]](#cite_note-Aftermath_(episode)-19)

 [![On worlds like Saleucami, clone troopers began to enforce new Imperial laws upon galactic citizens.](data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIABAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAEALAAAAAABAAEAQAICTAEAOw%3D%3D)](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/e/e0/ImperialInformationalStation-CaR.png/revision/latest?cb=20220102231414) [![On worlds like Saleucami, clone troopers began to enforce new Imperial laws upon galactic citizens.](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/e/e0/ImperialInformationalStation-CaR.png/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/250?cb=20220102231414)](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/e/e0/ImperialInformationalStation-CaR.png/revision/latest?cb=20220102231414) 

On worlds like Saleucami, clone troopers began to enforce new Imperial laws upon galactic citizens.

 

As the Empire spread, clone stormtroopers carried out the occupation and subjugation of former Separatist worlds[[75]](#cite_note-Common_Ground-75) and worlds ravaged by the Clone Wars.[[76]](#cite_note-Rescue_on_Ryloth-76) Rex, meanwhile, decided he needed to fight in the name of the Republic against the growing Imperial regime. Presumed dead by the Empire,[[26]](#cite_note-Battle_Scars-26) he took to working from the shadows[[27]](#cite_note-Rex-27) to strike against the Empire[[77]](#cite_note-Decommissioned-77) and to help any of his clone brothers who were outside the reach of the Imperial Military.[[27]](#cite_note-Rex-27) First, he traveled to Saleucami and warned clone deserter Cut Lawquane of the rising might of the Empire, leaving a mere day before Force 99 and Omega arrived to meet with Lawquane. Meanwhile, clone stormtroopers enforced the early Empire's introduction of the [chain code](/wiki/Chain_code "Chain code"), which contained the biometric details and criminal history of the Empire's citizens. Force 99 helped Lawquane and his family [escape](/wiki/Skirmish_at_Saleucami_town "Skirmish at Saleucami town") the Imperial-occupied Saleucami before departing themselves.[[43]](#cite_note-Cut_and_Run-43)

Elsewhere in the galaxy, clone trooper [Bellows](/wiki/Bellows_(clone_trooper) "Bellows (clone trooper)") found himself unaffected by Order 66 due to a head injury. Awoken from unconsciousness by [Lira Hardin](/wiki/Lira_Hardin "Lira Hardin"), Bellows discovered the fate of his fellow clones and instead elected to join the ranks of the [Xorrn Clan Assembly](/wiki/Clan_Assembly_(Xorrn) "Clan Assembly (Xorrn)").[[78]](#cite_note-Friends_Like_These-78) Also during the early Imperial period, clone shock troopers continued to patrol the upper levels of Coruscant[[79]](#cite_note-Dark_Lord_7-79) and even supported Darth Vader in his efforts to [capture](/wiki/Hunt_for_Jocasta_Nu "Hunt for Jocasta Nu") Jedi Master [Jocasta Nu](/wiki/Jocasta_Nu "Jocasta Nu"), the [Chief Librarian](/wiki/Chief_Librarian "Chief Librarian") of the [Jedi Archives](/wiki/Jedi_Archives "Jedi Archives").[[80]](#cite_note-Darth_Vader_10-80) In [19 BBY](/wiki/19_BBY "19 BBY"),[[81]](#cite_note-Dawn_Visual-81) [Cassian Jeron Andor](/wiki/Cassian_Jeron_Andor "Cassian Jeron Andor") witnessed clone stormtroopers occupy his home planet of [Ferrix](/wiki/Ferrix "Ferrix"), where the troopers were pelted with rocks by angry civilians. In retaliation, an [Imperial officer](/wiki/Unidentified_Imperial_officer_(Ferrix) "Unidentified Imperial officer (Ferrix)") ordered a rank of clones to aim their weapons in the direction of the protestors.
