As a result of the incident, Cassian's [adoptive father](/wiki/Andor_family "Andor family"), [Clem Andor](/wiki/Clem_Andor "Clem Andor"), was [publicly hanged](/wiki/Hanging "Hanging") despite his efforts to deescalate the situation.[[82]](#cite_note-Announcement-82)

#### Moving to terminate the program[]

:   [![icon](data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIABAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAEALAAAAAABAAEAQAICTAEAOw%3D%3D)](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/0/04/Blue_Glass_Arrow.svg/revision/latest?cb=20090726033133) Main article: [Project War-Mantle](/wiki/Project_War-Mantle "Project War-Mantle")

:   "*The clone trooper program is a cost prohibitive relic of the past, but until the time is right, it will continue to serve a purpose.*"
:   ―Wilhuff Tarkin[[21]](#cite_note-Replacements-21)

 [![Recruited through Project War-Mantle, the Elite Squad was the vanguard of a new generation of soldiers that ultimately replaced the clone troopers.](data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIABAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAEALAAAAAABAAEAQAICTAEAOw%3D%3D)](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/b/b0/The-Replacements.png/revision/latest?cb=20220105010821) [![Recruited through Project War-Mantle, the Elite Squad was the vanguard of a new generation of soldiers that ultimately replaced the clone troopers.](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/b/b0/The-Replacements.png/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/250?cb=20220105010821)](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/b/b0/The-Replacements.png/revision/latest?cb=20220105010821) 

Recruited through Project War-Mantle, the Elite Squad was the vanguard of a new generation of soldiers that ultimately replaced the clone troopers.

 

Despite Lama Su's continued insistence that clone troopers were superior to recruited soldiers, possessing superior skills as a result of their training, Tarkin still considered the Kaminoan cloning operation a costly endeavor. While Tarkin was concerned with the cost quality of clones, Rampart's interest lay in the loyalty of recruits who voluntarily joined the [Imperial Military](/wiki/Imperial_Military "Imperial Military"). Tarkin sanctioned the formation of a team of [Elite Squad Troopers](/wiki/Elite_Squad_Trooper "Elite Squad Trooper"); four non-clone volunteers recruited from across the galaxy, they were placed under the command of Crosshair, who remained loyal to the Empire. Rampart believed that [Crosshair's Elite Squad](/wiki/Elite_Squad "Elite Squad") could be trained to be just as effective as the clone troopers who served the Republic if given proper instruction by experienced clones. Their [first mission](/wiki/Mission_to_Onderon_(Elite_Squad) "Mission to Onderon (Elite Squad)") as a unit was against Gerrera's fighters, the same mission Clone Force 99 had refused to carry out, as an opportunity to prove the project's usefulness to Tarkin.[[21]](#cite_note-Replacements-21)

The Elite Squad returned to Kamino after killing the group of [insurgents](/wiki/Partisans "Partisans") and civilians they found on [Onderon](/wiki/Onderon "Onderon"). Despite the death of [ES-01](/wiki/ES-01 "ES-01"), who was executed for refusing to comply with the clone's order to kill unarmed prisoners, Tarkin considered the mission a success not only for the Empire, but [Project War-Mantle](/wiki/Project_War-Mantle "Project War-Mantle") as well. The Imperial officers' determination to replace clones with volunteer and conscripted soldiers caused Lama Su to fear for the future of Kamino and its cloning facilities. Their situation was compounded by the degradation of the last genetic samples of Jango Fett; therefore, Lama Su instructed Nala Se to continue her experiments in the hope of yielding a superior clone. He believed that the Kaminoans' relationship with the Empire hinged on the fate of the clone trooper program.[[21]](#cite_note-Replacements-21) At some point, Crosshair also had his inhibitor chip removed but continued to serve the Empire, having decided it was what he truly believed in.[[83]](#cite_note-Return_to_Kamino-83)

 [![Trained by clone commandos, TK stormtroopers were recruited from across the galaxy as eventual replacements for clone troopers.](data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIABAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAEALAAAAAABAAEAQAICTAEAOw%3D%3D)](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/4/4c/EmpireMilitary-WM.png/revision/latest?cb=20220116063841) [![Trained by clone commandos, TK stormtroopers were recruited from across the galaxy as eventual replacements for clone troopers.](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/4/4c/EmpireMilitary-WM.png/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/250?cb=20220116063841)](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/4/4c/EmpireMilitary-WM.png/revision/latest?cb=20220116063841) 

Trained by clone commandos, TK stormtroopers were recruited from across the galaxy as eventual replacements for clone troopers.

 

With Project War-Mantle's effectiveness proven through the victory on Onderon,[[21]](#cite_note-Replacements-21) an [Imperial training facility](/wiki/Imperial_Base_on_Daro "Imperial Base on Daro") was established on the planet [Daro](/wiki/Daro "Daro"). The facility contained a thousand non-clone "[TK stormtroopers](/wiki/TK_stormtrooper "TK stormtrooper")," who were recruited from across the galaxy and trained by the elite [clone commandos](/wiki/Clone_commando "Clone commando") like commando [Gregor](/wiki/Gregor "Gregor"). Gregor later commented that, while the TK troopers would not be as skilled as their predecessors, there were many of them, further alleging that the clones were being removed from the Imperial Military because they were created to serve the Republic, not the newly-established Empire.[[73]](#cite_note-War-Mantle-73) Aware of Tarkin's promise to soon suspend Kamino's cloning contracts, Kaminoans Lama Su and Nala Se hoped to create a superior clone template to secure their business relationship with the Empire. However, the continued deterioration of Jango Fett's remaining DNA samples convinced Su to point their resources at capturing Omega.[[21]](#cite_note-Replacements-21) Se hired[[84]](#cite_note-Cornered-84) the rising bounty hunter [Fennec Shand](/wiki/Fennec_Shand "Fennec Shand")[[85]](#cite_note-Rampage-85) to hunt Omega,[[84]](#cite_note-Cornered-84) secretly ordering her to keep Omega safe from Su instead of returning her to Kamino.[[18]](#cite_note-Bounty_Lost-18)

 [![On Bracca, clone troopers served alongside new Imperial recruits in their attempt to apprehend Clone Force 99.](data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIABAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAEALAAAAAABAAEAQAICTAEAOw%3D%3D)](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/7/70/BadBatchImperialArmy.png/revision/latest?cb=20220109221717) [![On Bracca, clone troopers served alongside new Imperial recruits in their attempt to apprehend Clone Force 99.](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/7/70/BadBatchImperialArmy.png/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/250?cb=20220109221717)](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/7/70/BadBatchImperialArmy.png/revision/latest?cb=20220109221717) 

On Bracca, clone troopers served alongside new Imperial recruits in their attempt to apprehend Clone Force 99.

 

As Project War-Mantle continued, clone stormtroopers and Elite Squad Troopers began to serve alongside each other in certain operations.[[86]](#cite_note-Reunion-86) When Rex reunited with Clone Force 99 and brought them to the scrap world of [Bracca](/wiki/Bracca "Bracca") so they could remove their behavioral modification biochips once and for all, members of the [Scrapper Guild](/wiki/Scrapper_Guild "Scrapper Guild") spotted the rogue clones and reported them to the Empire,[[26]](#cite_note-Battle_Scars-26) which had branded Clone Force 99 enemies of the state for their defection. Ignoring Su's suggestion to bring Clone Force 99 in alive due to their skill set, Rampart gave Crosshair permission to [hunt down](/wiki/Mission_on_Bracca "Mission on Bracca") his former squad with a combined force of clone troopers and his Elite Squad. Arriving after Rex's departure, the joint-clone and Elite Trooper force nearly wiped out the so-called Bad Batch, but they ultimately managed to escape. However, still believing Se's hunter was working to return Omega to Kamino, Su grew impatient and hired[[86]](#cite_note-Reunion-86) famed bounty hunter[[87]](#cite_note-Databank_Cad_Bane-87) [Cad Bane](/wiki/Cad_Bane "Cad Bane") to bring her in.[[86]](#cite_note-Reunion-86) Followed by both Shand and Clone Force 99, Bane lost custody of Omega after arriving at the Kaminoans' abandoned [cloning facility](/wiki/Bora_Vio_cloning_facility "Bora Vio cloning facility") in the [Lido system](/wiki/Lido_system "Lido system").[[18]](#cite_note-Bounty_Lost-18)

 [![On Ryloth, a Clone Captain named Howzer inspired a handful of his fellow clones to defy Imperial orders, leading to their imprisonment by Elite Squad Troopers.](data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIABAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAEALAAAAAABAAEAQAICTAEAOw%3D%3D)](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/d/d1/HowzerIncitesRebellion-RoR.png/revision/latest?cb=20220114050339) [![On Ryloth, a Clone Captain named Howzer inspired a handful of his fellow clones to defy Imperial orders, leading to their imprisonment by Elite Squad Troopers.](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/d/d1/HowzerIncitesRebellion-RoR.png/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/250?cb=20220114050339)](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/d/d1/HowzerIncitesRebellion-RoR.png/revision/latest?cb=20220114050339) 

On Ryloth, a Clone Captain named Howzer inspired a handful of his fellow clones to defy Imperial orders, leading to their imprisonment by Elite Squad Troopers.

 

Escaping Bane and Shand, Omega returned to Clone Force 99.[[18]](#cite_note-Bounty_Lost-18) While the group resumed their mercenary work to make their way in the Imperial-controlled galaxy, they began to use stun shots against the clone stormtroopers they encountered[[75]](#cite_note-Common_Ground-75) after their journey with Rex proved to them that the control chips within their brothers forced them to obey the Empire against their will.[[26]](#cite_note-Battle_Scars-26) Meanwhile, Crosshair and his Elite Squad joined a [clone battalion](/wiki/Lessu_battalion "Lessu battalion") on the former battleground of [Ryloth](/wiki/Ryloth "Ryloth") to enforce Imperial control, only for the appearance of Clone Force 99 to [destroy](/wiki/Rescue_on_Ryloth "Rescue on Ryloth") an entire Imperial refinery and free political prisoner [Cham Syndulla](/wiki/Cham_Syndulla "Cham Syndulla"). Convinced that Clone Force 99 was a threat, Rampart once again gave Crosshair permission to hunt down his former squad.[[76]](#cite_note-Rescue_on_Ryloth-76)

#### Decommissioning the program[]

:   "*This facility's being decommissioned. You don't seem too concerned.*"  
    "*Why would I be?*"  
    "*Because the Empire will be phasing out clones next.*"  
    "*Not the ones that matter.*"
:   ―Hunter and an overconfident Crosshair[[83]](#cite_note-Return_to_Kamino-83)

Eventually, commando Gregor decided to desert from the Imperial ranks rather than continuing to serve as an instructor for the clones' replacements on Daro. Pointed to the facility by Rex, Clone Force 99 [broke into](/wiki/Extraction_on_Daro "Extraction on Daro") the base to rescue Gregor. Hunter, the leader of Clone Force 99, was surprised by the TK soldiers' quality given that their instructors were clone commandos. Gregor admitted to not teaching the TK troopers everything he knew, regarding that it was the smart choice to hold back in their training. While he also affirmed TK troopers would not be as skilled as clones, Gregor further noted that the troopers made up for their shortcomings through their great number; numerous galactic citizens were willing to join with the Empire[[73]](#cite_note-War-Mantle-73) they believed had saved them from the Clone Wars.[[84]](#cite_note-Cornered-84) However, Hunter declared that their numbers would not be enough in every situation a soldier encountered.[[73]](#cite_note-War-Mantle-73)

 [![The Empire initiated an operation to decommission the cloning facility after canceling its contracts with Kamino.](data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIABAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAEALAAAAAABAAEAQAICTAEAOw%3D%3D)](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/9/9c/KaminoansandClones-WM.png/revision/latest?cb=20220116064255) [![The Empire initiated an operation to decommission the cloning facility after canceling its contracts with Kamino.](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/9/9c/KaminoansandClones-WM.png/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/250?cb=20220116064255)](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/9/9c/KaminoansandClones-WM.png/revision/latest?cb=20220116064255) 

The Empire initiated an operation to decommission the cloning facility after canceling its contracts with Kamino.

 

Concurrent to the incident on Daro, the Empire terminated Kamino's contracts. Rampart oversaw the [operation](/wiki/Attack_on_Kamino "Attack on Kamino") to remove of all essential personnel and equipment from Tipoca City, including every viable clone developed by the Kaminoans. Nala Se assured a group of clone cadets that they would still fulfill their purpose by becoming soldiers, despite their removal from the cloning facility. While Nala Se had assumed that the Kaminoan government would secure new clients given their success with the clone army, which was known throughout the galaxy, Lama Su reflected on the differences between the Republic and the Empire. He concluded that the operation on Kamino could not survive under the New Order, convinced that the Empire would destroy the Kaminoans rather than allowing them to continue their work without Imperial supervision. The Prime Minister planned his own evacuation from Kamino along with its most skilled scientists in the hope of ensuring their survival and the continuation of their program, but his plan was discovered by Rampart.[[73]](#cite_note-War-Mantle-73)

Although the Vice Admiral was not overly impressed by Nala Se's creations, he regarded her as a talented scientist nonetheless, one whose skills made her an asset to the Empire.[[73]](#cite_note-War-Mantle-73) As such, Se was taken into Imperial custody,[[83]](#cite_note-Return_to_Kamino-83) while Su was left to the mercy of the Elite Squad Troopers when Rampart declared the Empire did not need the politician.[[73]](#cite_note-War-Mantle-73) Tipoca City was virtually abandoned by the time Hunter, who was captured on Daro, was taken back to Kamino by Crosshair. Noting the presence of TK troopers carrying out the final stages of the withdrawal instead of clones, Hunter realized that the cloning facility was in the process of being decommissioned, and he warned Crosshair that their brethren would eventually be phased out of service as well. Aware of the Empire's plans, Crosshair was confident that only the "regs" would be replaced, whereas the elite units would continue to serve the Empire as soldiers.[[83]](#cite_note-Return_to_Kamino-83)

 [![After removing the Kaminoan technology in Tipoca City, the Empire destroyed the facility where the clone troopers were made.](data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIABAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAEALAAAAAABAAEAQAICTAEAOw%3D%3D)](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/c/c2/VenatorsDestroyTipocaCity-RtK.png/revision/latest?cb=20250503183858) [![After removing the Kaminoan technology in Tipoca City, the Empire destroyed the facility where the clone troopers were made.](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/c/c2/VenatorsDestroyTipocaCity-RtK.png/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/250?cb=20250503183858)](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/c/c2/VenatorsDestroyTipocaCity-RtK.png/revision/latest?cb=20250503183858) 

After removing the Kaminoan technology in Tipoca City, the Empire destroyed the facility where the clone troopers were made.

 

The other members of Clone Force 99 also returned to Kamino in an effort to [rescue](/wiki/Rescue_of_Hunter "Rescue of Hunter") their commanding officer, leading to their confrontation with Crosshair. During the firefight, Tarkin authorized the bombardment of the Kaminoan capital after Rampart reported that the cloning technology was firmly under Imperial control. His *Venator*-class Star Destroyers, still operated by a clone personnel, opened fire on the abandoned facility, resulting in the destruction of Tipoca City.[[83]](#cite_note-Return_to_Kamino-83) All other Kaminoan facilities across the planet were targeted as well, resulting in the complete annihilation of the Kaminoan cloning enterprise,[[88]](#cite_note-Kamino_Lost-88) just as Su had predicted.[[73]](#cite_note-War-Mantle-73) A [clone stormtrooper](/wiki/Unidentified_clone_trooper_(VZ-114) "Unidentified clone trooper (VZ-114)") aboard Rampart's Venator reported the success of the eradication;[[88]](#cite_note-Kamino_Lost-88) despite the control chips within the clones compelling them to obey Imperial orders,[[83]](#cite_note-Return_to_Kamino-83) the admission that the clones had destroyed their homes audibly hurt for the trooper to admit.[[88]](#cite_note-Kamino_Lost-88)

Clone Force 99, meanwhile, escaped the devastation of Kamino alive, but they again parted ways with Crosshair when their brother declared he would stay with the Empire, with or without his control chip. Nala Se was escorted from Kamino by an elite detachment of clone commandos[[88]](#cite_note-Kamino_Lost-88) known as the [Imperial royal guard](/wiki/Imperial_royal_guard "Imperial royal guard"),[[89]](#cite_note-KL_EG-89) who were distinct[[88]](#cite_note-Kamino_Lost-88) from the Emperor's red guard that some clones hoped to join to escape decommissioning.[[3]](#cite_note-Dark_Lord_2-3) Se was brought to the facility of [Mount Tantiss](/wiki/Mount_Tantiss "Mount Tantiss") on the planet [Wayland](/wiki/Wayland "Wayland"), where the Empire hoped to use her cloning expertise for future projects.[[89]](#cite_note-KL_EG-89) Despite the destruction of Kamino and the ongoing arrangements within the Empire for their eventual replacement,[[90]](#cite_note-Season_2_Date-90) clone stormtroopers continued to serve the Imperial regime.[[91]](#cite_note-Spoils_of_War-91)

#### The Imperial Defense Recruitment Bill[]

:   "*After all the clones have done… all we sacrificed. We're good soldiers. We followed orders. And for what?*"
:   ―Clone Commander [Mayday](/wiki/Mayday "Mayday")[[92]](#cite_note-The_Outpost-92)

 [![Gradually, TK stormtrooper recruits would continually integrate into the Imperial Army, slowly phasing out clone troopers.](data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIABAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAEALAAAAAABAAEAQAICTAEAOw%3D%3D)](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/b/b9/ImperialInspectorateCafeteria.png/revision/latest?cb=20230117205404) [![Gradually, TK stormtrooper recruits would continually integrate into the Imperial Army, slowly phasing out clone troopers.](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/b/b9/ImperialInspectorateCafeteria.png/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/250?cb=20230117205404)](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/b/b9/ImperialInspectorateCafeteria.png/revision/latest?cb=20230117205404) 

Gradually, TK stormtrooper recruits would continually integrate into the Imperial Army, slowly phasing out clone troopers.

 

Several months after the destruction of the Kaminoan facilities, which had been covered up as being the result of a cataclysmic storm, the [Imperial Senate](/wiki/Imperial_Senate "Imperial Senate") begun a vote on the [Imperial Defense Recruitment Bill](/wiki/Imperial_Defense_Recruitment_Bill "Imperial Defense Recruitment Bill"), which would formalize the Imperial Military's transition from a clone army to a volunteer-based force. While many senators such as [Gani Riduli](/wiki/Gani_Riduli "Gani Riduli") of the [InterGalactic Banking Clan](/wiki/InterGalactic_Banking_Clan "InterGalactic Banking Clan") greatly supported the idea of the bill, there was stiff opposition to it by several others. Senator [Riyo Chuchi](/wiki/Riyo_Chuchi "Riyo Chuchi") chiefly led the opposition to the bill, claiming that the clones did not deserve to be cast aside after their years of military service. While Admiral Rampart assured Chuchi that the clones would be compensated and given pensions for their service after retirement, the senator remained skeptical.[[93]](#cite_note-The_Clone_Conspiracy-93)

Alongside rogue Clone Captain Rex and Clone Force 99, Chuchi would begin working to expose Rampart for his involvement with the destruction of the Kaminoan facilities in an effort the stop the bill from passing. As the Bad Batch infiltrated Rampart's personal *Venator*, which was docked at the Coruscant Imperial Shipyards for maintenance and repairs, to retrieve the vessel's command log, Chuchi attempted to buy the squad time in the [Senate Building](/wiki/Imperial_Senate_Building "Imperial Senate Building"). After the squad had successfully extracted the command log and delivered it to the Senate Building, Chuchi revealed the footage of Rampart's fleet bombarding Kamino.[[94]](#cite_note-Truth_and_Consequences-94)

 [![Clone shock troopers arrest Vice Admiral Rampart, who Emperor Palpatine would use as a scapegoat to achieve Senate approval for the new stormtrooper program.](data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIABAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAEALAAAAAABAAEAQAICTAEAOw%3D%3D)](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/9/9c/TruthAndConsequences-Rampart.png/revision/latest?cb=20250111005542) [![Clone shock troopers arrest Vice Admiral Rampart, who Emperor Palpatine would use as a scapegoat to achieve Senate approval for the new stormtrooper program.](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/9/9c/TruthAndConsequences-Rampart.png/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/250?cb=20250111005542)](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/9/9c/TruthAndConsequences-Rampart.png/revision/latest?cb=20250111005542) 

Clone shock troopers arrest Vice Admiral Rampart, who Emperor Palpatine would use as a scapegoat to achieve Senate approval for the new stormtrooper program.

 

As the Senate erupted into chaos, Emperor Palpatine appeared to denounce Rampart's actions and have him publicly arrested. Despite condemning Rampart before the Senate, Palpatine also expressed shock at the actions of the clones under his command, who blindly followed orders without hesitation. Palpatine further exclaimed that the Empire should be led into a new era under the protection of non-clone Imperial stormtroopers. Following a thunderous applause, the Senate then approved the recruitment bill.[[94]](#cite_note-Truth_and_Consequences-94) While clone troopers continued to serve the Imperial Military for the time being,[[92]](#cite_note-The_Outpost-92) the passage of the bill allowed[[94]](#cite_note-Truth_and_Consequences-94) a growing number of clones to be decommissioned[[56]](#cite_note-The_Summit-56) by force. Such actions were framed as the clones entering "retirement,"[[92]](#cite_note-The_Outpost-92) a term that suggested a far more cozy fate than what awaited.[[74]](#cite_note-BB_S2-74) Having been soldiers all their lives[[93]](#cite_note-The_Clone_Conspiracy-93) and then being suddenly ousted from the military,[[92]](#cite_note-The_Outpost-92) some clones came to find themselves destitute.[[95]](#cite_note-Clone_Veteran-95) Other clones, meanwhile, found themselves secretly made into test subjects for the Empire's [Advanced Science Division](/wiki/Advanced_Science_Division "Advanced Science Division") upon being forced out of service.[[56]](#cite_note-The_Summit-56)

#### Further service and eventual retirement[]

The drop in casualties following the end of the war[[36]](#cite_note-Collapse-36) and the passing of the Defense Recruitment Bill[[94]](#cite_note-Truth_and_Consequences-94) allowed the Empire to suspend clone production without a major disruption in manpower as new, non-clone recruits would eventually take up the mantle.[[36]](#cite_note-Collapse-36) Nevertheless, the Empire continued to make use of clones throughout its formative years[[82]](#cite_note-Announcement-82) as they were gradually phased out of service,[[3]](#cite_note-Dark_Lord_2-3) with some units joining the ranks of the Emperor's [bodyguards](/wiki/Bodyguard "Bodyguard").[[8]](#cite_note-TSWB-8)

 [![Clone stormtroopers projected Imperial authority across the galaxy, using punitive measures to control the populations of occupied worlds.](data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIABAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAEALAAAAAABAAEAQAICTAEAOw%3D%3D)](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/9/93/Andor-Clones-on-Ferrix.png/revision/latest?cb=20221025202315) [![Clone stormtroopers projected Imperial authority across the galaxy, using punitive measures to control the populations of occupied worlds.](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/9/93/Andor-Clones-on-Ferrix.png/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/250?cb=20221025202315)](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/9/93/Andor-Clones-on-Ferrix.png/revision/latest?cb=20221025202315) 

Clone stormtroopers projected Imperial authority across the galaxy, using punitive measures to control the populations of occupied worlds.

 

Around a year into the Imperial Era, the Empire had already begun deploying natural-born[[45]](#cite_note-Ahsoka-45) conscripts and volunteers into the Stormtrooper Corps,[[21]](#cite_note-Replacements-21) but former-Jedi Ahsoka Tano assumed that clones would still be part of its ranks.[[45]](#cite_note-Ahsoka-45) Around the same year,[[96]](#cite_note-Date-96) a small force of clones stationed on [Barton IV](/wiki/Barton_IV "Barton IV") were replaced by enlisted stormtroopers after their numbers had been whittled down from insurgent attacks.[[92]](#cite_note-The_Outpost-92) The Imperial [Advanced Science Division](/wiki/Advanced_Science_Division "Advanced Science Division") continued to make extensive use of clone commandos, who formed the clandestine organization's elite [royal guard](/wiki/Imperial_royal_guard "Imperial royal guard"), and guarded its assets and facilities. The division also trained and deployed [clone X troopers](/wiki/Clone_X_trooper "Clone X trooper"), who served as highly fanatical [assassins](/wiki/Assassin "Assassin") for the Empire.[[97]](#cite_note-Metamorphosis_(episode)-97)

 [![In 15 BBY, clone stormtroopers would arrest the future Grand Admiral Thrawn while serving under Captain Parck.](data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIABAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAEALAAAAAABAAEAQAICTAEAOw%3D%3D)](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/e/e1/CaptiveThrawn-Thrawn1.png/revision/latest?cb=20180218041728) [![In 15 BBY, clone stormtroopers would arrest the future Grand Admiral Thrawn while serving under Captain Parck.](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/e/e1/CaptiveThrawn-Thrawn1.png/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/200?cb=20180218041728)](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/e/e1/CaptiveThrawn-Thrawn1.png/revision/latest?cb=20180218041728) 

In 15 BBY, clone stormtroopers would arrest the future Grand Admiral Thrawn while serving under Captain Parck.

 

Around [15 BBY](/wiki/15_BBY "15 BBY"),[[98]](#cite_note-15_BBY_Date-98) several squads of clone stormtroopers[[99]](#cite_note-Thrawn_1-99) were deployed on an [unidentified planet](/wiki/Unidentified_planet_(Thrawn%27s_exile) "Unidentified planet (Thrawn's exile)") during an operation in [Wild Space](/wiki/Wild_Space "Wild Space"), far away from the Core.[[100]](#cite_note-Thrawn_novel-100) The clones were still donned in their Phase II clone trooper armor, but had come to wield [E-11 medium blaster rifles](/wiki/E-11_medium_blaster_rifle "E-11 medium blaster rifle") and worked alongside non-clone [Imperial Navy Troopers](/wiki/Imperial_Navy_Trooper "Imperial Navy Trooper").[[99]](#cite_note-Thrawn_1-99) Nevertheless, as the years passed, the remaining clones were gradually rotated out of military service due to their rapid aging process.[[101]](#cite_note-A_New_Dawn_Panel-101) In addition, Imperial propaganda created an influx of non-clone recruits in the Imperial Military, accelerating the replacement of clones in the military. The clones, having fulfilled the main purpose for which they were created and trained to complete, were no longer needed by the Emperor. As a result, most clones quietly retired as they aged, but their legacy endured through the soldiers who replaced them.[[8]](#cite_note-TSWB-8) No longer using fresh clones to replenish the army due to the shutdown of the cloning hatcheries on Kamino,[[3]](#cite_note-Dark_Lord_2-3) the Imperial military transitioned from a clone army to a volunteer and conscription-based force.[[52]](#cite_note-Propaganda-52)

The clone stormtrooper known as Sergeant [Crest](/wiki/Crest "Crest") was still serving the Empire[[102]](#cite_note-Tarkin-102) in [14 BBY](/wiki/14_BBY "14 BBY"),[[103]](#cite_note-14_BBY_Chronology_Note-103) but Darth Vader initially considered the clone too old to remain on active duty due to his accelerated aging. However, Vader later promoted Crest to the rank of lieutenant.[[102]](#cite_note-Tarkin-102) Imperial clone shock troopers continued to patrol the streets of Coruscant[[104]](#cite_note-Dark_Lord_20-104) at least until 14 BBY,[[105]](#cite_note-Vader_18_Chronology_Note-105) where they assisted Vader in [hunting down](/wiki/Coruscant_Incident "Coruscant Incident") two rogue [Inquisitors](/wiki/Inquisitor "Inquisitor").[[104]](#cite_note-Dark_Lord_20-104)

 [![TX-828 "Torrent" was one of the last clones grown from the genetic template of Jango Fett.](data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIABAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAEALAAAAAABAAEAQAICTAEAOw%3D%3D)](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/c/cb/Torrent-SWI.jpg/revision/latest?cb=20190215071349) [![TX-828 "Torrent" was one of the last clones grown from the genetic template of Jango Fett.](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/c/cb/Torrent-SWI.jpg/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/180?cb=20190215071349)](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/c/cb/Torrent-SWI.jpg/revision/latest?cb=20190215071349) 

TX-828 "Torrent" was one of the last clones grown from the genetic template of Jango Fett.

 

By [4 BBY](/wiki/4_BBY "4 BBY"), most clones had been decommissioned and were regarded as obsolete.[[106]](#cite_note-The_Lost_Commanders-106) A small number of clones remained in Imperial service, acting as training instructors for the next generation of stormtroopers,[[107]](#cite_note-Lost_Commanders_Recon-107) but such a position did not guarantee the clones would like their cadets; clone trooper [Lassar](/wiki/Lassar "Lassar") resented enlisted recruits despite becoming an instructor.[[108]](#cite_note-TK-108) Another clone was [Torrent](/wiki/Torrent "Torrent"), who worked under the operating number TX-828; as one of the last clones in the [Stormtrooper Corps](/wiki/Stormtrooper_Corps "Stormtrooper Corps"), he was a rare sight by the time of the [Battle of Yavin](/wiki/Battle_of_Yavin "Battle of Yavin"). At that time he was nearing the age of forty due to his accelerated growth process, with strands of gray coloring his black hair. By then the rarity of Torrent's kind was such that [ISB](/wiki/Imperial_Security_Bureau "Imperial Security Bureau") [Senior Commander](/wiki/Senior_Commander "Senior Commander") [Alecia Beck](/wiki/Alecia_Beck "Alecia Beck") was surprised to encounter a stormtrooper from the original Kaminoan production line.[[109]](#cite_note-Smuggler's_Run-109)

An Imperial clone stormtrooper known as [Crag](/wiki/Crag "Crag") remained in military service well into the Empire's reign,[[110]](#cite_note-Born_in_the_Storm-110) despite his accelerated age.[[4]](#cite_note-Episode_II-4) The old clone had a strong sense of duty, which he believed was maintaining order in the galaxy. However, his personality earned the ire of a fellow trooper, [Sardis Ramsin](/wiki/Sardis_Ramsin "Sardis Ramsin"), who regarded Crag as a "relic." Crag was serving as a [sandtrooper](/wiki/Desert_stormtrooper "Desert stormtrooper") of [Foot Patrol 7](/wiki/Foot_Patrol_7 "Foot Patrol 7") when his team deployed to [Mos Eisley](/wiki/Mos_Eisley "Mos Eisley") on Tatooine,[[110]](#cite_note-Born_in_the_Storm-110) shortly before the Battle of [Yavin](/wiki/Yavin_Prime "Yavin Prime"). They had been sent to capture two droids belonging to the Rebellion, [C-3PO](/wiki/C-3PO "C-3PO") and [R2-D2](/wiki/R2-D2 "R2-D2"), but fell under the influence of a Jedi [mind trick](/wiki/Mind_trick "Mind trick") performed by an old [hermit](/wiki/Hermit "Hermit"). Unbeknownst to Crag and his team,[[110]](#cite_note-Born_in_the_Storm-110) the old man with the droids was the Jedi fugitive Obi-Wan Kenobi, who used the Force to dominate the weak-minded troopers in order to move the droids into the city unopposed.[[111]](#cite_note-Episode_IV-111)

### Legacy[]

#### Life after retirement[]

:   "*What's the point of all this? I mean, why?*"  
    "*I don't know, sir. I don't think anybody knows. But I* do *know that someday this war is gonna end.*"  
    "*Then what? We're soldiers. What happens to us then?*"
:   ―Rex and Fives during the war[[35]](#cite_note-Carnage_of_Krell-35)

 [![The remaining Fett clones eventually entered "retirement" due to their accelerated growth and gradual replacement by birth-born recruits, leaving many to live hard lives once the war they were made for was over.](data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIABAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAEALAAAAAABAAEAQAICTAEAOw%3D%3D)](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/e/e8/Homeless-clone-PartII.png/revision/latest?cb=20220706011224) [![The remaining Fett clones eventually entered "retirement" due to their accelerated growth and gradual replacement by birth-born recruits, leaving many to live hard lives once the war they were made for was over.](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/e/e8/Homeless-clone-PartII.png/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/300?cb=20220706011224)](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/e/e8/Homeless-clone-PartII.png/revision/latest?cb=20220706011224) 

The remaining Fett clones eventually entered "retirement" due to their accelerated growth and gradual replacement by birth-born recruits, leaving many to live hard lives once the war they were made for was over.

 

During the later years of the Clone Wars, many clones talked about retirement as a reward for their service, but few knew what it entailed. Indeed, the Republic planned to retire the clones, but neither the government nor the clones knew what that meant. If a soldier brought the subject up, their commander would often put an end to the idle chatter. A few forward-looking clones contemplated work in corporate security or consultation with local militaries owing to their lack of civilian job skills, and their accelerated aging process decreased the likelihood of them learning and mastering such job skills before they died. However, strong loyalties to the former Republic created a moral quandary when it came to security work, as retired clones would possibly be fighting some of their former brethren. Before the Republic collapsed, politicians had vetted certain officers about staying in a formalized and permanent Republic military to maintain the peace. A few exceptional clones had even been approached to run for political office.[[36]](#cite_note-Collapse-36)

Having proven their loyalty to the Republic, and with the civilian population loving military heroes, many clones would have made ideal candidates were it not for the clones' general disdain for politicking.[[36]](#cite_note-Collapse-36) Before her death at the end of the war, Senator [Padmé Amidala](/wiki/Padm%C3%A9_Amidala "Padmé Amidala") had drafted several bills concerning and advocating for clone personhood. The bills were amongst the works she hoped would be part of her legacy and included measures for personhood to be recognized during the war and after it. However, the drafts were effectively left abandoned after her death, although her loyal [handmaiden](/wiki/Naboo_Royal_Handmaidens "Naboo Royal Handmaidens") [Sabé](/wiki/Sab%C3%A9 "Sabé") had copies of the works.[[112]](#cite_note-Queen's_Shadow-112) The "retirement" offered by the Empire[[92]](#cite_note-The_Outpost-92) ultimately left many,[[113]](#cite_note-WinLose-113) eventually limited to a few, of the already-few surviving clones destitute.[[95]](#cite_note-Clone_Veteran-95) Despite the efforts of those in the Senate who supported clone rights[[56]](#cite_note-The_Summit-56) and the troopers' own service, no form of peaceful retirement had been prepared for the troopers.[[113]](#cite_note-WinLose-113) A number of veterans of the Clone Wars had a hard life. The Empire failed to keep up the [Crispus Commons](/wiki/Crispus_Commons "Crispus Commons") housing project on the planet [Gorse](/wiki/Gorse "Gorse")[[114]](#cite_note-A_New_Dawn-114) while [one 501st trooper](/wiki/Nax "Nax") was left homeless on the world of [Daiyu](/wiki/Daiyu "Daiyu"), where he begged for credits in a [city](/wiki/Daiyu_City "Daiyu City").[[115]](#cite_note-Part_II-115) A bounty hunter named [CT-720](/wiki/CT-720 "CT-720") was active during the Imperial Era.[[116]](#cite_note-Target_Vader_6-116)

#### Psychological impact of Order 66[]

:   "*The kid was right. Billaba was our* hero*. Yours and mine.*"  
    "*That traitor? No.* Never*!*"  
    "*Yes. She was. And* Order Sixty-Six*… We followed it—I followed it—as if under some kind of spell… As if I had no will of my own. No memories of the battles we had fought together. Not for* one second *did it occur to me to even* question *the Emperor's command!*"  
    "*Because when soldiers question orders, people die!*"  
    "*People died anyway! Master Billaba died at* my hands*! My friend, let's take one second now… Before it's too late.*"  
    "*You're talking like a Jedi traitor, Grey. We did what we had to do. Anything else is literally… Unthinkable.*"
:   ―Grey and Styles[[70]](#cite_note-TLP_5-70)

 [![Grey obediently executed Order 66, only to later question why he did so in the first place.](data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIABAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAEALAAAAAABAAEAQAICTAEAOw%3D%3D)](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/a/a4/Grey-gets-Order-66.png/revision/latest?cb=20211231051611) [![Grey obediently executed Order 66, only to later question why he did so in the first place.](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/a/a4/Grey-gets-Order-66.png/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/250?cb=20211231051611)](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/a/a4/Grey-gets-Order-66.png/revision/latest?cb=20211231051611) 

Grey obediently executed Order 66, only to later question why he did so in the first place.

 

Despite the Kaminoans' attempt at designing the clones to be beyond any form of combat-induced stress,[[57]](#cite_note-The_Unknown-57) the troopers ultimately could suffer from post-traumatic stress. Beyond clones developing post-traumatic stress from the war[[117]](#cite_note-MIA-117) and the deaths of their brothers,[[118]](#cite_note-The_Last_Battle-118) some clones were left traumatized by the aftereffects of Order 66, leaving them bitter and horrified at their actions.[[119]](#cite_note-HitFlix-119) On one occasion, [Grey](/wiki/Grey_(clone_trooper) "Grey (clone trooper)") was dismayed by his own thoughtless execution of Order 66—an experience which he described as being in trance, and therefore, unable to control his actions. Captain [Styles](/wiki/Styles "Styles") did not share his commander's concern over the moral issues of Order 66, however. In an effort to atone for his participation in the Jedi Purge, Grey sacrificed his life to save [Caleb Dume](/wiki/Kanan_Jarrus "Kanan Jarrus"), the apprentice of Jedi Master [Depa Billaba](/wiki/Depa_Billaba "Depa Billaba") whom the clone killed while under the influence of Order 66.[[70]](#cite_note-TLP_5-70) Another clone that expressed regret regarding his actions was Cody, who mentioned having difficulty living with his choices in a conversation with Crosshair. Later, Rampart tells Crosshair that Cody has disappeared.

Sometime after the issuing of Order 66[[9]](#cite_note-Shattered-9) and the removal of Rex's chip, [Wolffe](/wiki/Wolffe "Wolffe") and Gregor had their chips removed.[[120]](#cite_note-Shattered_Trivia-120) In the years that followed the Clone Wars, Rex and the other two clone veterans lived in retirement on [Seelos](/wiki/Seelos "Seelos"), where they made a home out of a modified [All Terrain Tactical Enforcer](/wiki/All_Terrain_Tactical_Enforcer "All Terrain Tactical Enforcer"). Despite the effects of their accelerated growth, the aging clones decided to oppose the Empire by joining the nascent rebellion, a movement dedicated to the restoration of the Republic that the clones once served. Regarding the clones' view of stormtroopers, Rex was generally dismissive of the humans who replaced his brethren.[[121]](#cite_note-Relics-121)

#### Galactic Empire[]

:   "*If it's a fight you want, I hope you brought a better class of soldier than those…*stormtroopers*.*"  
    "*They serve the Empire well, and I have* a great many of them*.*"  
    "*You're gonna need all of 'em.* "
:   ―Rex and [Alexsandr Kallus](/wiki/Alexsandr_Kallus "Alexsandr Kallus")[[121]](#cite_note-Relics-121)

 [![Republic propaganda inspired birth-born humans to follow the clone troopers' example by becoming Imperial stormtroopers.](data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIABAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAEALAAAAAABAAEAQAICTAEAOw%3D%3D)](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/2/2b/Unite.jpg/revision/latest?cb=20180131041145) [![Republic propaganda inspired birth-born humans to follow the clone troopers' example by becoming Imperial stormtroopers.](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/2/2b/Unite.jpg/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/200?cb=20180131041145)](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/2/2b/Unite.jpg/revision/latest?cb=20180131041145) 

Republic propaganda inspired birth-born humans to follow the clone troopers' example by becoming Imperial stormtroopers.

 

Although the clone trooper program was decommissioned under the Empire, their service in the Clone Wars inspired a generation of birth-born humans, both throughout the conflict and the years that followed. At the time there was no army to enlist in; save for the clones' Jedi Generals, the Grand Army of the Republic was exclusively based on a single template. The Republic faithful nevertheless wanted to do their part as citizens of the thousand-year democracy; as such, they were encouraged by COMPOR propaganda to [purchase war bonds](/wiki/Buy_Republic_War_Bonds "Buy Republic War Bonds") or [report acts of sedition](/wiki/Keep_Our_Republic_Secure "Keep Our Republic Secure") to the authorities.[[52]](#cite_note-Propaganda-52)

The [Commission for the Preservation of the New Order](/wiki/Commission_for_the_Preservation_of_the_New_Order "Commission for the Preservation of the New Order") (COMPNOR) built upon the carefully engineered symbols and messages of its COMPOR predecessor to accelerate the vast military expansion as decreed by Emperor Palpatine. For all of COMPOR's efforts to mythologize the clone troopers, portraying them as gallant heroes of the Republic in a barrage of propaganda, clones remained an abstraction in the public's mind. Yet whereas the Grand Army's ranks were exclusively clone-based, the galactic populace was [encouraged by COMPNOR](/wiki/Join "Join") to serve the state by doing more than purchasing bonds, reporting treason or [rationing supplies](/wiki/Assure_Our_Victory! "Assure Our Victory!"). With the cloning operation on Kamino suspended, ordinary citizens volunteered for military service in the hopes of wearing the armor of the Imperial stormtrooper and becoming heroes like the clone soldiers they idolized.[[52]](#cite_note-Propaganda-52)

The [first generation](/wiki/Dark_Trooper_(original) "Dark Trooper (original)") of [Dark Trooper](/wiki/Dark_Trooper "Dark Trooper") created under the Empire's [Dark Trooper project](/wiki/Dark_Trooper_project "Dark Trooper project") were clones given cybernetic augmentations, with over seventy percent of the clone's body being replaced by robotics.[[122]](#cite_note-Sideshow_Dark_Trooper-122) By the later years of the Galactic Empire, clone troopers and the Grand Army of the Republic were virtually forgotten, effectively becoming a lost generation of unappreciated veterans despite their valiant service.[[123]](#cite_note-Rebels_Recon_Lost-123) By the war's end, clones had saved billions of lives across the galaxy, while their vehicles and equipment inspired new weapons such as the [E-11 medium blaster rifle](/wiki/E-11_medium_blaster_rifle "E-11 medium blaster rifle"), based on the common clone weapon the [DC-15](/wiki/DC-15A_blaster_carbine "DC-15A blaster carbine").[[124]](#cite_note-DC-15-124)

#### Clones in the Rebellion[]

:   "*Tell me, what's it like to be a* traitor*?*"  
    "*I'm* no traitor*. You want an answer, ask the Emperor about it.*"  
    "*Don't you feel* guilty *for* turning *your* back *on the* Empire *and* joining *these* rebels*?*"  
    "*These "*rebels*" are* saving people's lives*, which is more than the Empire's been doing across the galaxy.*"
:   ―[Jeken](/wiki/Jeken "Jeken") and Rex[[125]](#cite_note-Academy_Cadets-125)

 [![Captain Rex went on to support the Alliance to Restore the Republic against the Galactic Empire.](data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIABAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAEALAAAAAABAAEAQAICTAEAOw%3D%3D)](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/e/ed/RexRebels-TSWB.png/revision/latest?cb=20211225211850) [![Captain Rex went on to support the Alliance to Restore the Republic against the Galactic Empire.](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/e/ed/RexRebels-TSWB.png/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/200?cb=20211225211850)](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/e/ed/RexRebels-TSWB.png/revision/latest?cb=20211225211850) 

Captain Rex went on to support the Alliance to Restore the Republic against the Galactic Empire.

 

Although the extensive majority of clone troopers were loyal to the Empire, held in place by training, a sense of duty, and established organic programming, a few clones were able to discover how to disconnect or repel their programming. Of those few, even fewer decided to rebel against the Empire, mostly due to their increasingly old age or situations. The rebellious clones brought their combat training and experience to the various resistance groups that they joined and were also knowledgeable in Imperial strategy and military bureaucracy. Although clones active in the growing rebellion operated apart from each other, some instances saw several clones working together.[[126]](#cite_note-Dawn-126)

At least one Jedi survivor harbored a grudge against the clones. Kanan Jarrus was traumatized by the events of Order 66, including the sudden execution of his Master, Depa Billaba by their own clone troopers, who betrayed and murdered the Jedi Master without hesitation. This experience caused him to develop a strong sense of bitterness toward the clones.[[106]](#cite_note-The_Lost_Commanders-106) Nonetheless, Jarrus and his apprentice [Ezra Bridger](/wiki/Ezra_Bridger "Ezra Bridger") helped Rex, Wolffe, and Gregor achieve [victory over Imperial forces](/wiki/Assault_on_Seelos "Assault on Seelos") on Seelos[[121]](#cite_note-Relics-121) after Ahsoka Tano urged them to recruit Rex to the rebellion.[[106]](#cite_note-The_Lost_Commanders-106) Their victory on Seelos forever proved that the clone troopers were superior soldiers to those who had replaced them.[[127]](#cite_note-Rex_Roll-127) Nonetheless, after Rex joined the rebellion, Jarrus still possessed his grudge for a time, but Jarrus came to respect and view him as a friend after the Captain nearly sacrificed himself for Jarrus. After the mission, Jarrus went as far as to salute the clone, which surprised Rex, but he quickly returned it.[[128]](#cite_note-Stealth_Strike-128) After the Rebellion fully formed into the [Alliance to Restore the Republic](/wiki/Alliance_to_Restore_the_Republic "Alliance to Restore the Republic"), Rex continued to serve, later being joined by Gregor and Wolffe for the [Liberation of Lothal](/wiki/Liberation_of_Lothal "Liberation of Lothal").[[129]](#cite_note-Family_Farewell-129)

Additionally, one of Wolffe's former troopers, [Wildfire](/wiki/Wildfire_(clone_trooper) "Wildfire (clone trooper)") happened to join the rebels, later learning that his former officer was amongst the organization. After learning about Wolffe's involvement with the Rebellion, Wildfire joined a [mission to Seelos](/wiki/Mission_to_Seelos "Mission to Seelos").[[130]](#cite_note-Tyrants-130) During the Liberation of [Lothal](/wiki/Lothal "Lothal"), Gregor was fatally shot by an [Imperial weapons technician](/wiki/Imperial_weapons_technician "Imperial weapons technician"). As he died, he thanked Rex for the chance to fight for a cause that they had chosen to believe in. Although he was saddened by Gregor's death, Rex continued to fight for the Rebels, eventually promoted to the rank of commander in the organization. He served in the [Battle of Endor](/wiki/Battle_of_Endor "Battle of Endor"),[[129]](#cite_note-Family_Farewell-129) which would prove to be a major loss for the Empire because of the deaths of Emperor Palpatine and Darth Vader.[[131]](#cite_note-Episode_VI-131)

#### New Republic Era[]

:   "*Of course I don't believe it! A clone that knows the location of forgotten Separatist treasures? Not only is that ridiculous, but the clones are extinct!*"
:   ―A [Devaronian](/wiki/Devaronian "Devaronian"), in [Takodana Castle](/wiki/Takodana_Castle "Takodana Castle")[[132]](#cite_note-Grand_Theft_Falcon-132)

 [![Kix was the last known surviving clone trooper.](data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIABAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAEALAAAAAABAAEAQAICTAEAOw%3D%3D)](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/6/65/Kix-TBB.png/revision/latest?cb=20200223053123) [![Kix was the last known surviving clone trooper.](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/6/65/Kix-TBB.png/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/180?cb=20200223053123)](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/6/65/Kix-TBB.png/revision/latest?cb=20200223053123) 

Kix was the last known surviving clone trooper.

 

The clones of Jango Fett were said to have been extinct by the time of the [New Republic Era](/wiki/New_Republic_Era "New Republic Era").[[132]](#cite_note-Grand_Theft_Falcon-132) Although Boba Fett stood apart from the other Jango Fett clones, being an unmodified clone,[[4]](#cite_note-Episode_II-4) he was still physically identical to them. His voice revealed him as a clone to [Bo-Katan Kryze](/wiki/Bo-Katan_Kryze "Bo-Katan Kryze"), who recognized Boba's voice inflection and tone as that of his donor, having heard the late Jango through thousands of clone troopers.[[133]](#cite_note-Chapter_16-133)

At least [one clone trooper](/wiki/Sconto%27s_father "Sconto's father") was said to have sired a child before dying in the Clone Wars. [Sconto](/wiki/Sconto "Sconto"), according to [his mother](/wiki/Sconto%27s_mother "Sconto's mother"), was the son of that clone. Unlike the clone, Sconto aged at a normal rate and was living as a [merchant](/wiki/Merchant "Merchant") in Utapau's [Pau City](/wiki/Pau_City "Pau City")—the site of one of the final battles in the Clone Wars[[134]](#cite_note-Force_Collector-134)—about [thirty-two years](/wiki/32_ABY "32 ABY")[[135]](#cite_note-Sconto_Year-135) after the Battle of Yavin. Sconto was proud of his heritage and therefore harbored resentment toward the Jedi, whom he held responsible for his father's death.[[134]](#cite_note-Force_Collector-134)

[Kix](/wiki/Kix "Kix"), a clone trooper of the 501st Legion, was discovered by the [pirate](/wiki/Pirate "Pirate") [Sidon Ithano](/wiki/Sidon_Ithano "Sidon Ithano") over fifty years after the end of the Clone Wars. At the time, Ithano located a downed Separatist vessel and decided to raid it, assuming he would find valuable [kyber crystals](/wiki/Kyber_crystal "Kyber crystal") once belonging to Count Dooku. Instead, he found Kix, who had been frozen in stasis since the late Clone Wars, because he had discovered Order 66. The [clone medic](/wiki/Clone_medic "Clone medic") was deeply saddened when he learned about the end of the Republic and the loss of his brothers, and ultimately joined [Ithano's crew](/wiki/Sidon_Ithano%27s_pirate_crew "Sidon Ithano's pirate crew") due to his expertise in Clone Wars-era technology and the knowledge he possessed regarding the locations of former military locations.[[136]](#cite_note-Crimson_Corsair-136)

#### First Order[]

:   "*How capable are your soldiers, General?*"  
    "*I won't have you question my methods.*"  
    "*They're obviously skilled at committing high treason. Perhaps Leader Snoke should consider using a clone army.*"
:   ―Kylo Ren and Armitage Hux[[137]](#cite_note-Episode_VII-137)

 [![The legacy of clone troopers influenced stormtroopers for generations, from the Galactic Empire to the First Order.](data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIABAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAEALAAAAAABAAEAQAICTAEAOw%3D%3D)](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/4/4a/First_Order_Stormtrooper_Corps.jpg/revision/latest?cb=20230726034603) [![The legacy of clone troopers influenced stormtroopers for generations, from the Galactic Empire to the First Order.](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/4/4a/First_Order_Stormtrooper_Corps.jpg/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/280?cb=20230726034603)](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/4/4a/First_Order_Stormtrooper_Corps.jpg/revision/latest?cb=20230726034603) 

The legacy of clone troopers influenced stormtroopers for generations, from the Galactic Empire to the First Order.

 

Among military circles, the clones were remembered for their effectiveness.[[137]](#cite_note-Episode_VII-137) Determined to reclaim the Imperial legacy,[[138]](#cite_note-First_Order-138) the [First Order](/wiki/First_Order "First Order") initiated a [clandestine project](/wiki/Project_Resurrection "Project Resurrection") that centered on conscripting human children into its [forces](/wiki/First_Order_military "First Order military").[[139]](#cite_note-Battlefront_II-139) Trained in live-fire drills and programmed through First Order propaganda, they became the [new generation of stormtroopers](/wiki/First_Order_stormtrooper "First Order stormtrooper").[[140]](#cite_note-FO-Stormtroopers-140) As the latest iteration of one of the most distinctive symbols of military might in the galaxy,[[141]](#cite_note-TLJ:TVD-141) First Order stormtroopers wore [stark white armor](/wiki/First_Order_stormtrooper_armor "First Order stormtrooper armor") derived from that of their Imperial predecessors and the Republic clone troopers who came before them.[[140]](#cite_note-FO-Stormtroopers-140)

Though General [Armitage Hux](/wiki/Armitage_Hux "Armitage Hux") had complete confidence in his soldiers, convinced they were well trained and programmed, his rival [Kylo Ren](/wiki/Ben_Solo "Ben Solo") doubted their loyalty to the First Order and [Supreme Leader](/wiki/Supreme_Leader "Supreme Leader") [Snoke](/wiki/Snoke "Snoke"). During the [Cold War](/wiki/Cold_War "Cold War") with the [New Republic](/wiki/New_Republic "New Republic"), Ren accused Hux's stormtroopers of harboring the potential for treason after [FN-2187](/wiki/Finn "Finn") betrayed the First Order. The [dark warrior](/wiki/Knights_of_Ren "Knights of Ren") suggested that a clone army would be more reliable, using the rogue trooper as an [example](/wiki/Escape_from_the_Finalizer "Escape from the Finalizer") of a flaw that was potentially systemic to the stormtrooper program. The general responded to Ren's criticism by assuring him that the stormtroopers were exceptionally reliable in their combat skills and allegiance to the First Order.[[137]](#cite_note-Episode_VII-137)

 [![Sith troopers were the culmination of decades spent creating an army programmed for absolute loyalty.](data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIABAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAEALAAAAAABAAEAQAICTAEAOw%3D%3D)](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/4/4e/Sith_trooper_trio.png/revision/latest?cb=20191225041713) [![Sith troopers were the culmination of decades spent creating an army programmed for absolute loyalty.](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/4/4e/Sith_trooper_trio.png/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/250?cb=20191225041713)](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/4/4e/Sith_trooper_trio.png/revision/latest?cb=20191225041713) 

Sith troopers were the culmination of decades spent creating an army programmed for absolute loyalty.

 

At the height of the [First Order-Resistance War](/wiki/First_Order-Resistance_War "First Order-Resistance War"), the [Sith Eternal](/wiki/Sith_Eternal "Sith Eternal") [cult](/wiki/Religion "Religion") readied an army of elite soldiers to support the First Order's ultimate push toward galactic conquest. Though they were named after a revived sect of the dark side, [Sith troopers](/wiki/Sith_trooper "Sith trooper") were the culmination of decades that the Empire spent attempting to strip individuality from its soldiers. Molding individual beings into fervently loyal extensions of the Emperor's will was a process that experienced much trial and error since the Clone Wars. Darth Sidious was dismayed to discover that clone troopers exhibited disconcerting amounts of free will despite their genetically engineered background and numerous alterations. While the Sith troopers were not clones, they underwent flash-imprinting and loyalty conditioning built upon and advanced beyond the Kaminoan procedures of earlier generations. As a result, they were far more loyal and machine-like than the First Order's trained-from-childhood stormtroopers.[[142]](#cite_note-TROS_VD-142)

## Training[]

:   "*I want you troopers to remember—we're shoulder-to-shoulder on those front lines. Brothers! And sometimes we may quarrel, but no matter what, we are* united*. Rule one: we fight together.*"
:   ―"[Colt](/wiki/Colt "Colt")"[[143]](#cite_note-CloneCadets-143)

 [![Clone troopers were rigorously trained on Kamino to become the elite soldiers of the Galactic Republic.](data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIABAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAEALAAAAAABAAEAQAICTAEAOw%3D%3D)](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/d/d2/Training_Room_Kamino_AtG.png/revision/latest?cb=20190416143537) [![Clone troopers were rigorously trained on Kamino to become the elite soldiers of the Galactic Republic.](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/d/d2/Training_Room_Kamino_AtG.png/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/250?cb=20190416143537)](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/d/d2/Training_Room_Kamino_AtG.png/revision/latest?cb=20190416143537) 

Clone troopers were rigorously trained on Kamino to become the elite soldiers of the Galactic Republic.

 

In order to rapidly produce a large army, the clones were subscribed to an accelerated training and aging program. All clones went through painful accelerated growth before reaching maturity, all while enduring nonstop training, simulations, and testing. Letter and number identifications were assigned to the clones to remove any sense of identity, as the cloners and trainers on Kamino viewed them as pieces of a machine, and not people. Endless mental and physical drills bled into the clones' "recreation," where they participated in sports and games that resembled battle situations. Any bouts of anger or rebellion were dealt with by placing clones in retraining pods, essentially isolation tanks. Throughout their time on Kamino, their engineers muttered veiled threats of "disposal" if the clones failed their testing. As the war progressed, the Jedi clamped down on the more egregious attitudes, but the engineers of Kamino maintained their view of the clones as merely a product.[[36]](#cite_note-Collapse-36)

 [![Young clones went through intense classes, with alternating odd and even helmets.](data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIABAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAEALAAAAAABAAEAQAICTAEAOw%3D%3D)](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/a/a6/Youngclonestraining.jpg/revision/latest?cb=20070815200125) [![Young clones went through intense classes, with alternating odd and even helmets.](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/a/a6/Youngclonestraining.jpg/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/250?cb=20070815200125)](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/a/a6/Youngclonestraining.jpg/revision/latest?cb=20070815200125) 

Young clones went through intense classes, with alternating odd and even helmets.

 

Clone education was very rapid, and their learning consisted of intense classes that used screens and focus-enhancing helmets to help clones memorize information that might have one day been useful on the battlefield. Young clones were assigned to wear either an "odd-class" or an "even-class" helmet, in order to foster a sense of teamwork and competitiveness. Helmets that had gold-fittings were "odd-class," and helmets that had black fittings were "even-class."[[144]](#cite_note-CVD_New_Edition-144)

As trainees, clones held the rank of [clone cadet](/wiki/Clone_cadet "Clone cadet") and were organized into multiple [squads](/wiki/Squad "Squad") for the purpose of learning cooperation and teamwork.[[143]](#cite_note-CloneCadets-143) Cadets had several kinds of instructors; younger clones were monitored by full-grown clone sergeants[[145]](#cite_note-DeathTrap-145) and bounty hunters were hired to supervise the older clones. If a clone was unable to complete training, they could be assigned to [maintenance duty](/wiki/Maintenance_duty_clone "Maintenance duty clone"). By the time of the Clone Wars, Jedi Master Shaak Ti personally oversaw the training of new generations of clone troopers. ARC troopers were also assigned to inspect the progress of future troopers.[[143]](#cite_note-CloneCadets-143) Clones deemed exceptional in comparison to the average, rank-and-file trooper,[[146]](#cite_note-ARCTroopers-146) were given specialized training in order to become elite soldiers, such as [clone commandos](/wiki/Clone_commando "Clone commando")[[147]](#cite_note-TheBadBatch-147) or ARC troopers.[[146]](#cite_note-ARCTroopers-146)

 [![The clone trooper training program was overseen by mercenaries and battle-experienced clones.](data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIABAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAEALAAAAAABAAEAQAICTAEAOw%3D%3D)](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/1/1b/Arcbricscrubber.png/revision/latest?cb=20130505041445) [![The clone trooper training program was overseen by mercenaries and battle-experienced clones.](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/1/1b/Arcbricscrubber.png/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/250?cb=20130505041445)](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/1/1b/Arcbricscrubber.png/revision/latest?cb=20130505041445) 

The clone trooper training program was overseen by mercenaries and battle-experienced clones.

 

During the war, Shaak Ti observed how some cadets, such as [Domino Squad](/wiki/Domino_Squad "Domino Squad"), struggled to complete their training. Lama Su, who regarded the Domino clones as sub-standard units, believed they were the result of the Kaminoans' need to stretch their remaining supply of Jango Fett's DNA due to the template's untimely demise on Geonosis. The prime minister also opined that a new genotype would have to be selected in order to produce more clones fit for combat.[[143]](#cite_note-CloneCadets-143)

The clones lived and trained in [Tipoca City](/wiki/Tipoca_City "Tipoca City"), the capital [city](/wiki/City "City") of Kamino, throughout their time as [cadets](/wiki/Cadet "Cadet").[[4]](#cite_note-Episode_II-4) Naturally, clones came to regard Kamino as their homeworld, just as official records did. Training and studying under the soft white lights of the clone facilities, most never saw the rain, oceans, clouds, or sky until they left for combat. Still, from the moment of their birth, the clones received encouragement from their trainers and genetic engineers to leave Kamino, and become soldiers among the stars.[[36]](#cite_note-Collapse-36)

At least two clone squads were given a tour of the *Venator*-class Star Destroyer *[Endurance](/wiki/Endurance "Endurance")* during the Clone Wars as part of the [Clone Youth Brigade](/wiki/Clone_Youth_Brigade "Clone Youth Brigade"). The point of this on-site training exercise was to test the cadets' knowledge regarding the functions and layout of a Star Destroyer. It was also meant to help prepare the cadets for their future as fully trained clone troopers.[[145]](#cite_note-DeathTrap-145)

 [!["Shiny" was a slang term for novice clone troopers who finished their training, but were lacking in battle experience.](data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIABAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAEALAAAAAABAAEAQAICTAEAOw%3D%3D)](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/7/74/Rookies-EpisodeGuideThumbnail.jpg/revision/latest?cb=20211005104816) [!["Shiny" was a slang term for novice clone troopers who finished their training, but were lacking in battle experience.](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/7/74/Rookies-EpisodeGuideThumbnail.jpg/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/250?cb=20211005104816)](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/7/74/Rookies-EpisodeGuideThumbnail.jpg/revision/latest?cb=20211005104816) 

"Shiny" was a slang term for novice clone troopers who finished their training, but were lacking in battle experience.

 

The clones who failed to complete their training were disqualified from becoming soldiers. Instead of military service, failed clones—such as [99](/wiki/Clone_99 "Clone 99")—were given janitorial duties and menial work. The cadets who succeeded in their trials were promoted to active duty.[[143]](#cite_note-CloneCadets-143) Despite the status of trooper, a novice clone trooper was regarded as a rookie or "[shiny](/wiki/Shiny "Shiny")" by the older, more battle-experienced clones. If a clone survived his first battle, he was no longer considered a shiny but rather a full-fledged soldier of the Republic.[[148]](#cite_note-Rookies-148)

Ahsoka Tano felt as though the clones knew battle in their very [blood](/wiki/Blood "Blood"),[[45]](#cite_note-Ahsoka-45) while trooper Fives once proclaimed that a clone's training was in his blood.[[146]](#cite_note-ARCTroopers-146) Clones were taught [Galactic Basic Standard](/wiki/Galactic_Basic_Standard "Galactic Basic Standard"), the language of the Galactic Republic. Those who spent a lot of time stationed on a specific planet could adopt a patois of the local language. Clones tended to litter their speech with jargon and slang—such as "[clankers](/wiki/List_of_phrases_and_slang#C "List of phrases and slang")" for droids—incomprehensible to a civilian or a Jedi unfamiliar with military culture.[[36]](#cite_note-Collapse-36)

As the war progressed, command allowed clones to pursue hobbies within limited parameters to supplement their off-duty training and improve mental health. This improved morale and recovery; however, it also gave clones insight into the "other side" and how the civilian population lived.[[36]](#cite_note-Collapse-36)

## Equipment[]

:   "*Generation one armor always holds up.*"
:   ―Rex[[118]](#cite_note-The_Last_Battle-118)

[Phase I clone trooper armor](/wiki/Phase_I_clone_trooper_armor "Phase I clone trooper armor") was the first version in the [clone trooper armor](/wiki/Clone_trooper_armor "Clone trooper armor") series. It was issued to clone troopers on Kamino prior to the Clone Wars,[[4]](#cite_note-Episode_II-4) and was in service until it was rendered obsolete by [Phase II](/wiki/Phase_II_clone_trooper_armor "Phase II clone trooper armor") around the time of the [Battle of Mon Cala](/wiki/Battle_of_Mon_Cala "Battle of Mon Cala").[[149]](#cite_note-WaterWar-149) Both versions of clone trooper [armor](/wiki/Armor "Armor") could be modified with an array of attachments, such as [jetpacks](/wiki/Jetpack "Jetpack")[[33]](#cite_note-TCWFilm-33) and [macrobinoculars](/wiki/Macrobinoculars "Macrobinoculars").[[2]](#cite_note-Episode_III-2) To better monitor ground movements and coordinate attacks, all clone troopers held a tracking device within their helmets that allowed controllers on [*Acclamator*-class transgalactic military assault ships](/wiki/Acclamator-class_transgalactic_military_assault_ship "Acclamator-class transgalactic military assault ship") to better monitor the combat zone.[[150]](#cite_note-SOTG-150)

 [![Phase II clone trooper armor was worn by clones, replacing Phase I at the height of the Clone Wars.](data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIABAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAEALAAAAAABAAEAQAICTAEAOw%3D%3D)](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/7/7b/Clone_trooper_armor.png/revision/latest?cb=20141223035439) [![Phase II clone trooper armor was worn by clones, replacing Phase I at the height of the Clone Wars.](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/7/7b/Clone_trooper_armor.png/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/250?cb=20141223035439)](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/7/7b/Clone_trooper_armor.png/revision/latest?cb=20141223035439) 

Phase II clone trooper armor was worn by clones, replacing Phase I at the height of the Clone Wars.

 

At first, Phase I armor used color to distinguish clones trained for leadership roles, such as [captains](/wiki/Captain "Captain") and commanders, from each other and the standard troopers in the Grand Army of the Republic.[[4]](#cite_note-Episode_II-4) As the Clone Wars progressed, color gradually became used for the purpose of armor customization and unit identification.[[33]](#cite_note-TCWFilm-33) The trend was maintained during the service of Phase II armor,[[2]](#cite_note-Episode_III-2) but was ultimately discarded by the time of the creation of [stormtrooper armor](/wiki/Stormtrooper_armor "Stormtrooper armor") after the Clone Wars.[[151]](#cite_note-SparkOfRebellion-151) The identifying white armor of both Phases signified an honorable symbol of defense; however, the creation of the stormtrooper skewed this symbolism into one of a faceless icon of conformity.[[152]](#cite_note-TFAVD-152)

Clone troopers were armed with the [DC-15A blaster rifle](/wiki/DC-15A_blaster_rifle "DC-15A blaster rifle") and [DC-15A blaster carbine](/wiki/DC-15A_blaster_carbine "DC-15A blaster carbine") for long-ranged combat,[[4]](#cite_note-Episode_II-4) as well as the [DC-17 repeater hand blaster](/wiki/DC-17_repeater_hand_blaster "DC-17 repeater hand blaster") for short-ranged combat.[[153]](#cite_note-Blaster_Pistol-153) They also wielded several types of [grenades](/wiki/Grenade "Grenade"), including [Electro Magnetic Pulse grenades](/wiki/Electromagnetic_pulse_grenade "Electromagnetic pulse grenade")[[154]](#cite_note-Innocents-154) and [thermal detonators](/wiki/Thermal_detonator "Thermal detonator").[[155]](#cite_note-R2ComeHome-155)

With the exception of the Coruscant Guard's red-armored shock troopers,[[19]](#cite_note-Aftermath_(episode)-19) the clone troopers who served the Galactic Empire restored their Phase II armor to its standard white appearance.[[67]](#cite_note-Aftermath_Episode_Guide-67) Under the leadership of the Jedi, color was used to distinguish the various units in the Grand Army of the Republic, allowing clones to express their individuality with the Jedi's encouragement.[[68]](#cite_note-Clone_Armor_DB-68) Returning to a force of white-armored soldiers symbolized the loss of the Jedi's influence and the individualism of the clones, replaced by programmed conformity.[[67]](#cite_note-Aftermath_Episode_Guide-67)

## Specialized clone troopers[]

 [![The Kaminoan emblem was worn by all clones.](data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIABAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAEALAAAAAABAAEAQAICTAEAOw%3D%3D)](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/e/e6/Clone_cadet.svg/revision/latest?cb=20250718095412) [![The Kaminoan emblem was worn by all clones.](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/e/e6/Clone_cadet.svg/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/180?cb=20250718095412)](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/e/e6/Clone_cadet.svg/revision/latest?cb=20250718095412) 

The Kaminoan emblem was worn by all clones.

 

To fill the demand of the different situations that occur during wartime, various clone troopers received extra or specialized training. The battles took place in many different environments during the Clone Wars and as such, the need for specialized gear also arose.[[156]](#cite_note-Armor_Gallery-156)

* **[Advanced Recon Commandos](/wiki/Advanced_Recon_Commando "Advanced Recon Commando")** — Also known as ARC troopers, elite clone troopers that excel and received further training.[[156]](#cite_note-Armor_Gallery-156)
* **[Advanced Recon Force Scout Troopers](/wiki/Advanced_Recon_Force_trooper "Advanced Recon Force trooper")** — Also known as ARF troopers, clone troopers who specialized in stealth, and trained to pilot the [All Terrain Reconnaissance Transport](/wiki/All_Terrain_Reconnaissance_Transport "All Terrain Reconnaissance Transport"); equipped with light armor.[[156]](#cite_note-Armor_Gallery-156)
* **[Biker Advanced Recon Commandos](/wiki/Biker_Advanced_Recon_Commando "Biker Advanced Recon Commando")** — Also known as BARC troopers, clone troopers equipped to use [BARC speeders](/wiki/BARC_speeder "BARC speeder").[[156]](#cite_note-Armor_Gallery-156)
* **[Clone artillery troopers](/wiki/Clone_artillery_trooper "Clone artillery trooper")** — Clone troopers that formed three-man teams to operate [mortars](/wiki/Mortar "Mortar").[[15]](#cite_note-Rise-15)
* **[Clone cold assault troopers](/wiki/Clone_cold_assault_trooper "Clone cold assault trooper")** — Clone troopers equipped with cold weather gear to be able to operate in frigid environments.[[156]](#cite_note-Armor_Gallery-156)

 [![The clone commando was an elite class of soldier in the Grand Army of the Republic.](data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIABAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAEALAAAAAABAAEAQAICTAEAOw%3D%3D)](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/7/70/Clone_Commando_Battlefront_2.jpg/revision/latest?cb=20200403143414) [![The clone commando was an elite class of soldier in the Grand Army of the Republic.](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/7/70/Clone_Commando_Battlefront_2.jpg/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/250?cb=20200403143414)](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/7/70/Clone_Commando_Battlefront_2.jpg/revision/latest?cb=20200403143414) 

The clone commando was an elite class of soldier in the Grand Army of the Republic.

 

* **[Clone commandos](/wiki/Clone_commando "Clone commando")** — Clone troopers specially bred by the Kaminoans to be the elite force of the Grand Army; received specialized training and equipment.[[156]](#cite_note-Armor_Gallery-156)
* **[Clone Comms Technicians](/wiki/Clone_Comms_Technician "Clone Comms Technician")** — Specialized clones equipped with communications equipment that were responsible for allowing proper communication within a military unit.[[157]](#cite_note-Republic_Specialists-157)
* **[Clone Engineers](/wiki/Clone_Engineer "Clone Engineer")** — Specialized clone troopers who served as [engineers](/wiki/Engineer "Engineer") and were responsible for maintaining vehicles in top condition.[[157]](#cite_note-Republic_Specialists-157)
* **[Clone flametroopers](/wiki/Clone_flametrooper "Clone flametrooper")** — Specialized clone troopers with fire resistant armor and flamethrowers.[[156]](#cite_note-Armor_Gallery-156)
* **[Clone gunners](/wiki/Clone_gunner "Clone gunner")** — Clone troopers equipped to man [AV-7 Anti-vehicle Artillery Cannons](/wiki/AV-7_Anti-vehicle_Artillery_Cannon "AV-7 Anti-vehicle Artillery Cannon")[[156]](#cite_note-Armor_Gallery-156) and other [artillery](/wiki/Artillery "Artillery") pieces, including those aboard starships.[[145]](#cite_note-DeathTrap-145)
* **[Clone jetpack troopers](/wiki/Clone_jetpack_trooper "Clone jetpack trooper")** — Clone troopers equipped with a [jetpack](/wiki/Jetpack "Jetpack") and [missile launcher](/wiki/Missile_launcher "Missile launcher").[[139]](#cite_note-Battlefront_II-139)
* **[Clone trooper officers](/wiki/Clone_trooper_officer "Clone trooper officer")** — Clone troopers that served as officers.[[158]](#cite_note-The_Hidden_Enemy-158)
  + **[Clone medical officers](/wiki/Clone_medical_officer "Clone medical officer")** — Clone trooper officers that have specialized medical roles.[[159]](#cite_note-Ultimate_Star_Wars-159)
  + **[Clone navigation officers](/wiki/Clone_navigation_officer "Clone navigation officer")** — Clone trooper officers who assisted in crewing starships in the Republic Navy.[[33]](#cite_note-TCWFilm-33)
* **[Clone medics](/wiki/Clone_medic "Clone medic")** — Clone troopers that served as medics.[[39]](#cite_note-The_Deserter-39)  [![The clone ordnance specialist was trained in bomb defusal.](data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIABAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAEALAAAAAABAAEAQAICTAEAOw%3D%3D)](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/1/15/Squad_Clone_Trooper_Ordnance_Specialist_-_Sideshow.png/revision/latest?cb=20160818192902) [![The clone ordnance specialist was trained in bomb defusal.](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/1/15/Squad_Clone_Trooper_Ordnance_Specialist_-_Sideshow.png/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/150?cb=20160818192902)](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/1/15/Squad_Clone_Trooper_Ordnance_Specialist_-_Sideshow.png/revision/latest?cb=20160818192902) 

  The clone ordnance specialist was trained in bomb defusal.
* **[Clone ordnance specialists](/wiki/Clone_ordnance_specialist "Clone ordnance specialist")** — Clone troopers that have received specialized training in arming and defusing bombs.[[156]](#cite_note-Armor_Gallery-156)
* **[Clone paratroopers](/wiki/Clone_paratrooper "Clone paratrooper")** — Clone troopers trained for airborne assaults.[[156]](#cite_note-Armor_Gallery-156)
* **[Clone riot troopers](/wiki/Riot_clone_trooper "Riot clone trooper")** — Clone troopers with specialized riot control training.[[160]](#cite_note-DuchessofMandalore-160)
* **[Clone scout troopers](/wiki/Clone_scout_trooper "Clone scout trooper")** — Clone troopers with light armor and trained in reconnaissance.[[156]](#cite_note-Armor_Gallery-156)
* **[Clone SCUBA troopers](/wiki/Clone_SCUBA_trooper "Clone SCUBA trooper")** — Clone troopers equipped with aquatic armor and weaponry.[[156]](#cite_note-Armor_Gallery-156)
* **[Clone shadow troopers](/wiki/Clone_shadow_trooper "Clone shadow trooper")** — Clone troopers who were the predecessors of the Imperial [shadow troopers](/wiki/Shadow_trooper "Shadow trooper").[[161]](#cite_note-FC_4S-161)
* **[Clone sharpshooters](/wiki/Clone_sharpshooter "Clone sharpshooter")** — Clone troopers trained to be [snipers](/wiki/Sniper "Sniper").[[162]](#cite_note-FA-162)
* **[Clone shock troopers](/wiki/Imperial_shock_trooper "Imperial shock trooper")** — Clone troopers bred especially for the [Coruscant Guard](/wiki/Coruscant_Guard "Coruscant Guard").[[163]](#cite_note-CoruscantGuard-163)
* **[Clone trooper flight crews](/wiki/Clone_trooper_flight_crew "Clone trooper flight crew")** — Clone troopers that have received specialized training in ship maintenance.[[164]](#cite_note-TVE-164)
