* **[Clone trooper pilots](/wiki/Clone_trooper_pilot "Clone trooper pilot")** — Clone troopers bred to pilot starfighters and other vehicles; equipped with specialized armor.[[156]](#cite_note-Armor_Gallery-156)
  + **AT-TE Drivers** — Clone pilots who controlled [All Terrain Tactical Enforcers](/wiki/All_Terrain_Tactical_Enforcer "All Terrain Tactical Enforcer").[[165]](#cite_note-AT-TE_Driver-165)
* **[Clone X troopers](/wiki/Clone_X_trooper "Clone X trooper")** — Clones who were specialized[[166]](#cite_note-Truth_Slide_2-166) commando warriors active during the Imperial Era.[[167]](#cite_note-Clone_X-167)
* [**Dark Troopers**](/wiki/Dark_Trooper_(original) "Dark Trooper (original)")— the original iteration of the [Dark Trooper](/wiki/Dark_Trooper "Dark Trooper"), these [cyborg](/wiki/Cyborg "Cyborg") clone troopers had over seventy percent of their body replaced by mechanical components.[[122]](#cite_note-Sideshow_Dark_Trooper-122)
* **[Disguised Clone Troopers](/wiki/Disguised_Clone_Trooper "Disguised Clone Trooper")** — Clone troopers undercover as surviving Jedi after the siege of the Jedi Temple.[[168]](#cite_note-French_Novel-168)
* **[Heavy weapons clone troopers](/wiki/Heavy_weapons_clone_trooper "Heavy weapons clone trooper")** — Clone troopers equipped with stronger armor and [Z-6 rotary blaster cannons](/wiki/Z-6_rotary_blaster_cannon "Z-6 rotary blaster cannon").[[169]](#cite_note-Beginnings-169) Additionally, clone troopers that provided infantry with anti-vehicle support.[[170]](#cite_note-Galactic_Defense-170)
* **[Maintenance duty clones](/wiki/Maintenance_duty_clone "Maintenance duty clone")** — Clones who were unable to serve on the frontlines and were instead assigned a maintenance role.[[143]](#cite_note-CloneCadets-143)
* **[Special ops clone troopers](/wiki/Special_ops_clone_trooper "Special ops clone trooper")** — Clone troopers trained for stealth; equipped with advanced gear.[[156]](#cite_note-Armor_Gallery-156)
* **[Stealth clone pilots](/wiki/Stealth_clone_pilot "Stealth clone pilot")** — Clone troopers trained to pilot stealth ships; equipped with specialized armor.[[164]](#cite_note-TVE-164)

## Behind the scenes[]

The [Prequel trilogy](/wiki/Prequel_trilogy "Prequel trilogy") clone troopers were created through computer-generated imagery. In [*Star Wars*: Episode II *Attack of the Clones*](/wiki/Star_Wars:_Episode_II_Attack_of_the_Clones "Star Wars: Episode II Attack of the Clones"), the school-aged clones were played by [Daniel Logan](/wiki/Daniel_Logan "Daniel Logan"), the young adult versions by [Bodie Taylor](/wiki/Bodie_Taylor "Bodie Taylor"), and the mature versions by [Temuera Morrison](/wiki/Temuera_Morrison "Temuera Morrison"). Morrison also provided voiceover for all of the adult clone troopers.[[4]](#cite_note-Episode_II-4) For [*Star Wars*: Episode III *Revenge of the Sith*](/wiki/Star_Wars:_Episode_III_Revenge_of_the_Sith "Star Wars: Episode III Revenge of the Sith"), Morrison and Taylor both wore blue bodysuits while playing clone troopers with visible faces, such as [Cody](/wiki/Cody "Cody"), [Odd Ball](/wiki/Davijaan "Davijaan"), [Jag](/wiki/Jag "Jag"), and three [212th Attack Battalion](/wiki/212th_Attack_Battalion "212th Attack Battalion") members present during [Obi-Wan Kenobi](/wiki/Obi-Wan_Kenobi "Obi-Wan Kenobi")'s briefing (two played by Morrison in a close-up of Kenobi and Cody talking, the other by Taylor). Morrison and Taylor's bodysuits were later digitally replaced with computer-generated clone armor.[[2]](#cite_note-Episode_III-2) In addition to these on-screen appearances, Bodie Taylor is also depicted in a helmetless Phase I clone pilot stock image printed in several encyclopedias. Rather than taking a new photo of Taylor, the image was instead created by cutting Taylor's head from the pre-existing young adult clone stock image, and placing it onto the computer-generated pilot body.[[4]](#cite_note-Episode_II-4)

[Dee Bradley Baker](/wiki/Dee_Bradley_Baker "Dee Bradley Baker") voiced all of the clone troopers in *[Star Wars: The Clone Wars](/wiki/Star_Wars:_The_Clone_Wars "Star Wars: The Clone Wars")*[[158]](#cite_note-The_Hidden_Enemy-158) and *[Star Wars Rebels](/wiki/Star_Wars_Rebels "Star Wars Rebels")*,[[121]](#cite_note-Relics-121) while Daniel Logan reprised his role as the clone cadets in *The Clone Wars* episodes "[Death Trap](/wiki/Death_Trap "Death Trap")"[[145]](#cite_note-DeathTrap-145) and "[ARC Troopers](/wiki/ARC_Troopers_(episode) "ARC Troopers (episode)")."[[146]](#cite_note-ARCTroopers-146) For *The Clone Wars*, composter [Kevin Kiner](/wiki/Kevin_Kiner "Kevin Kiner") wrote the [clone fanfare](/wiki/Clone_fanfare "Clone fanfare") that acts as the clone trooper theme.[[171]](#cite_note-TCWS-171)

A clone trooper by the name of [Rattle](/wiki/Rattle "Rattle") was intended to appear in the novel *[Servants of the Empire: Edge of the Galaxy](/wiki/Servants_of_the_Empire:_Edge_of_the_Galaxy "Servants of the Empire: Edge of the Galaxy")* by [Jason Fry](/wiki/Jason_Fry "Jason Fry"), who described the character as a mentor to series protagonist [Zare Leonis](/wiki/Zare_Leonis "Zare Leonis"). However, Frey was told to remove the character because it was similar to a plot point in the then-upcoming [*Star Wars Rebels* Season Two](/wiki/Star_Wars_Rebels_Season_Two "Star Wars Rebels Season Two").[[172]](#cite_note-EotG_Notes_2-172) Within *Rebels*, Rex was re-introduced and became a mentor to the show's own protagonist, Ezra Bridger.[[173]](#cite_note-Brothers_Broken-173)

The [2019](/wiki/2019 "2019") [Fantasy Flight Games](/wiki/Fantasy_Flight_Games "Fantasy Flight Games") sourcebook *[Collapse of the Republic](/wiki/Collapse_of_the_Republic "Collapse of the Republic")* claims that, during their time training on Kamino, clone troopers had no time to form friendships with their cohort beyond a soldier's bond.[[36]](#cite_note-Collapse-36) However, *The Clone Wars* episode "[Clone Cadets](/wiki/Clone_Cadets "Clone Cadets")," which depicts Domino Squad during their training on the water world, establishes that clones already view each other as brothers during this time, with cadets Fives and [Echo](/wiki/Echo "Echo") going as far as to look out for each other by requesting a transfer.[[143]](#cite_note-CloneCadets-143) As *Collapse of the Republic* is only a roleplaying sourcebook, this article assumes "Clone Cadets" is correct. Another 2019 FFG sourcebook, *[Rise of the Separatists](/wiki/Rise_of_the_Separatists "Rise of the Separatists")*, stated that clones tended to view their fellow soldiers as family, fallen comrades as ancestors, and new recruits as descendants.[[15]](#cite_note-Rise-15) However, various other sources instead establish all clones view each other as siblings, no matter the age difference between them.[[45]](#cite_note-Ahsoka-45)[[145]](#cite_note-DeathTrap-145)[[148]](#cite_note-Rookies-148) Therefore, this article assumes *Rise of the Separatists* is incorrect.

[↑](#cite_ref-Databank_Cad_Bane_87-0) [StarWars-DatabankII](/wiki/Databank_(2014-) "Databank (2014-)") [Cad Bane](https://www.starwars.com/databank/cad-bane) in the [Databank](/wiki/Databank_(2014-) "Databank (2014-)") ([backup link](https://web.archive.org/web/20220209195219/https://www.starwars.com/databank/cad-bane)) 88. ↑ [88.0](#cite_ref-Kamino_Lost_88-0) [88.1](#cite_ref-Kamino_Lost_88-1) [88.2](#cite_ref-Kamino_Lost_88-2) [88.3](#cite_ref-Kamino_Lost_88-3) [88.4](#cite_ref-Kamino_Lost_88-4) [TBBtemplate](/wiki/Star_Wars:_The_Bad_Batch "Star Wars: The Bad Batch") *[Star Wars: The Bad Batch](/wiki/Star_Wars:_The_Bad_Batch "Star Wars: The Bad Batch")* — "[Kamino Lost](/wiki/Kamino_Lost "Kamino Lost")" 89. ↑ [89.0](#cite_ref-KL_EG_89-0) [89.1](#cite_ref-KL_EG_89-1) [StarWars.com](/wiki/StarWars.com "StarWars.com") ["Kamino Lost" Episode Guide | The Bad Batch](https://www.starwars.com/series/the-bad-batch/kamino-lost-episode-guide) on [StarWars.com](/wiki/StarWars.com "StarWars.com") ([backup link](https://web.archive.org/web/20210816130842/https://www.starwars.com/series/the-bad-batch/kamino-lost-episode-guide)) 90. [↑](#cite_ref-Season_2_Date_90-0) Per the reasoning [here](/wiki/Template:TruthAndConsequencesDate "Template:TruthAndConsequencesDate"), the seventh and eighth episodes of [*The Bad Batch* Season 2](/wiki/The_Bad_Batch_Season_2 "The Bad Batch Season 2"), "[The Clone Conspiracy](/wiki/The_Clone_Conspiracy "The Clone Conspiracy")" and "[Truth and Consequences](/wiki/Truth_and_Consequences "Truth and Consequences")," can be placed in [18 BBY](/wiki/18_BBY "18 BBY"). Therefore, all Season 2 episodes proceeding "The Clone Conspiracy" occur between [19 BBY](/wiki/19_BBY "19 BBY"), which features the end of [*The Bad Batch* Season 1](/wiki/The_Bad_Batch_Season_1 "The Bad Batch Season 1") according to *[Star Wars: Timelines](/wiki/Star_Wars:_Timelines "Star Wars: Timelines")*, and 18 [BBY](/wiki/%27ABY-BBY%27_dating_system "'ABY-BBY' dating system"). The [Galactic Empire](/wiki/Galactic_Empire "Galactic Empire"), the [formation](/wiki/Proclamation_of_the_New_Order "Proclamation of the New Order") of which *Star Wars: Timelines* dates to 19 BBY, sent [Mayday's squad](/wiki/Mayday%27s_squad "Mayday's squad") to [Barton IV](/wiki/Barton_IV "Barton IV") over a [year](/wiki/Standard_year "Standard year") prior to the events of the twelfth episode, "[The Outpost](/wiki/The_Outpost "The Outpost")." As it occurs over a year into the [Imperial Era](/wiki/Imperial_Era "Imperial Era") and is set shortly after the events of "Truth and Consequences," the events of "The Outpost" occur around 18 BBY. Following that logic, the ninth through eleventh episodes ("[The Crossing](/wiki/The_Crossing "The Crossing")" through "[Metamorphosis](/wiki/Metamorphosis_(episode) "Metamorphosis (episode)")") are also set around 18 BBY because they occur between the events of "Truth and Consequences" and "The Outpost." Finally, all season 2 episodes set after "The Outpost" occur shortly after its events, thereby placing those episodes around 18 BBY as well. 91. [↑](#cite_ref-Spoils_of_War_91-0) [TBBtemplate](/wiki/Star_Wars:_The_Bad_Batch "Star Wars: The Bad Batch") *[Star Wars: The Bad Batch](/wiki/Star_Wars:_The_Bad_Batch "Star Wars: The Bad Batch")* — "[Spoils of War](/wiki/Spoils_of_War "Spoils of War")" 92. ↑ [92.0](#cite_ref-The_Outpost_92-0) [92.1](#cite_ref-The_Outpost_92-1) [92.2](#cite_ref-The_Outpost_92-2) [92.3](#cite_ref-The_Outpost_92-3) [92.4](#cite_ref-The_Outpost_92-4) [92.5](#cite_ref-The_Outpost_92-5) [TBBtemplate](/wiki/Star_Wars:_The_Bad_Batch "Star Wars: The Bad Batch") *[Star Wars: The Bad Batch](/wiki/Star_Wars:_The_Bad_Batch "Star Wars: The Bad Batch")* — "[The Outpost](/wiki/The_Outpost "The Outpost")" 93. ↑ [93.0](#cite_ref-The_Clone_Conspiracy_93-0) [93.1](#cite_ref-The_Clone_Conspiracy_93-1) [TBBtemplate](/wiki/Star_Wars:_The_Bad_Batch "Star Wars: The Bad Batch") *[Star Wars: The Bad Batch](/wiki/Star_Wars:_The_Bad_Batch "Star Wars: The Bad Batch")* — "[The Clone Conspiracy](/wiki/The_Clone_Conspiracy "The Clone Conspiracy")" 94. ↑ [94.0](#cite_ref-Truth_and_Consequences_94-0) [94.1](#cite_ref-Truth_and_Consequences_94-1) [94.2](#cite_ref-Truth_and_Consequences_94-2) [94.3](#cite_ref-Truth_and_Consequences_94-3) [TBBtemplate](/wiki/Star_Wars:_The_Bad_Batch "Star Wars: The Bad Batch") *[Star Wars: The Bad Batch](/wiki/Star_Wars:_The_Bad_Batch "Star Wars: The Bad Batch")* — "[Truth and Consequences](/wiki/Truth_and_Consequences "Truth and Consequences")" 95. ↑ [95.0](#cite_ref-Clone_Veteran_95-0) [95.1](#cite_ref-Clone_Veteran_95-1) [StarWars-DatabankII](/wiki/Databank_(2014-) "Databank (2014-)") [Clone Veteran](https://www.starwars.com/databank/clone-veteran) in the [Databank](/wiki/Databank_(2014-) "Databank (2014-)") ([backup link](https://web.archive.org/web/20220805134620/https://www.starwars.com/databank/clone-veteran)) 96. [↑](#cite_ref-Date_96-0) Per the reasoning [here](/wiki/Template:TruthAndConsequencesDate "Template:TruthAndConsequencesDate"), the seventh and eighth episodes of [*The Bad Batch* Season 2](/wiki/The_Bad_Batch_Season_2 "The Bad Batch Season 2"), "[The Clone Conspiracy](/wiki/The_Clone_Conspiracy "The Clone Conspiracy")" and "[Truth and Consequences](/wiki/Truth_and_Consequences "Truth and Consequences")," can be placed in [18 BBY](/wiki/18_BBY "18 BBY"). Therefore, all Season 2 episodes proceeding "The Clone Conspiracy" occur between [19 BBY](/wiki/19_BBY "19 BBY"), which features the end of [*The Bad Batch* Season 1](/wiki/The_Bad_Batch_Season_1 "The Bad Batch Season 1") according to *[Star Wars: Timelines](/wiki/Star_Wars:_Timelines "Star Wars: Timelines")*, and 18 [BBY](/wiki/%27ABY-BBY%27_dating_system "'ABY-BBY' dating system"). The [Galactic Empire](/wiki/Galactic_Empire "Galactic Empire"), the [formation](/wiki/Proclamation_of_the_New_Order "Proclamation of the New Order") of which *Star Wars: Timelines* dates to 19 BBY, sent [Mayday's squad](/wiki/Mayday%27s_squad "Mayday's squad") to [Barton IV](/wiki/Barton_IV "Barton IV") over a [year](/wiki/Standard_year "Standard year") prior to the events of the twelfth episode, "[The Outpost](/wiki/The_Outpost "The Outpost")." As it occurs over a year into the [Imperial Era](/wiki/Imperial_Era "Imperial Era") and is set shortly after the events of "Truth and Consequences," the events of "The Outpost" occur around 18 BBY. Following that logic, the ninth through eleventh episodes ("[The Crossing](/wiki/The_Crossing "The Crossing")" through "[Metamorphosis](/wiki/Metamorphosis_(episode) "Metamorphosis (episode)")") are also set around 18 BBY because they occur between the events of "Truth and Consequences" and "The Outpost." Finally, all season 2 episodes set after "The Outpost" occur shortly after its events, thereby placing those episodes around 18 BBY as well. 97. [↑](#cite_ref-Metamorphosis_(episode)_97-0) [TBBtemplate](/wiki/Star_Wars:_The_Bad_Batch "Star Wars: The Bad Batch") *[Star Wars: The Bad Batch](/wiki/Star_Wars:_The_Bad_Batch "Star Wars: The Bad Batch")* — "[Metamorphosis](/wiki/Metamorphosis_(episode) "Metamorphosis (episode)")" 98. [↑](#cite_ref-15_BBY_Date_98-0) Chapter 19 of [*Thrawn*](/wiki/Thrawn_(novel) "Thrawn (novel)") includes [Arihnda Pryce](/wiki/Arihnda_Pryce "Arihnda Pryce") being appointed [governor of Lothal](/wiki/Governor_of_the_Lothal_sector "Governor of the Lothal sector"), which *[Star Wars: Timelines](/wiki/Star_Wars:_Timelines "Star Wars: Timelines")* dates to [11 BBY](/wiki/11_BBY "11 BBY"). As chapter 19 also establishes it has been approximately four [years](/wiki/Standard_year "Standard year") since the start of *Thrawn*, the novel must have began around [15 BBY](/wiki/15_BBY "15 BBY"). 99. ↑ [99.0](#cite_ref-Thrawn_1_99-0) [99.1](#cite_ref-Thrawn_1_99-1) [*Thrawn* 1](/wiki/Thrawn_1 "Thrawn 1") 100. [↑](#cite_ref-A_New_Dawn_Panel_101-0) [StarWars.com](/wiki/StarWars.com "StarWars.com") [SDCC 2014: *Star Wars: A New Dawn* Panel – Liveblog](https://www.starwars.com/news/sdcc-2014-star-wars-a-new-dawn-panel-liveblog) on [StarWars.com](/wiki/StarWars.com "StarWars.com") ([backup link](https://web.archive.org/web/20170805173938/https://www.starwars.com/news/sdcc-2014-star-wars-a-new-dawn-panel-liveblog)) 102. ↑ [102.0](#cite_ref-Tarkin_102-0) [102.1](#cite_ref-Tarkin_102-1) [*Tarkin*](/wiki/Tarkin_(novel) "Tarkin (novel)") 103. [↑](#cite_ref-14_BBY_Chronology_Note_103-0) *[Star Wars: Timelines](/wiki/Star_Wars:_Timelines "Star Wars: Timelines")* dates the events of [*Tarkin*](/wiki/Tarkin_(novel) "Tarkin (novel)") to [14 BBY](/wiki/14_BBY "14 BBY"). 104. ↑ [104.0](#cite_ref-Dark_Lord_20_104-0) [104.1](#cite_ref-Dark_Lord_20_104-1) [*Darth Vader* (2017) 20](/wiki/Darth_Vader_(2017)_20 "Darth Vader (2017) 20") 105. [↑](#cite_ref-Vader_18_Chronology_Note_105-0) *[Star Wars: Timelines](/wiki/Star_Wars:_Timelines "Star Wars: Timelines")* dates the events of [*Tarkin*](/wiki/Tarkin_(novel) "Tarkin (novel)") to [14 BBY](/wiki/14_BBY "14 BBY"). As [Darth Vader](/wiki/Anakin_Skywalker "Anakin Skywalker") knows about [Wilhuff Tarkin](/wiki/Wilhuff_Tarkin "Wilhuff Tarkin")'s past on [Eriadu](/wiki/Eriadu "Eriadu") in [*Darth Vader* (2017) 18](/wiki/Darth_Vader_(2017)_18 "Darth Vader (2017) 18"), which he only learned about in *Tarkin*, issue 18 must take place after the novel. The later issue [*Darth Vader* (2017) 19](/wiki/Darth_Vader_(2017)_19 "Darth Vader (2017) 19") featured the [Second Sister](/wiki/Second_Sister "Second Sister"), who was [killed](/wiki/Death "Death") in *[Star Wars Jedi: Fallen Order](/wiki/Star_Wars_Jedi:_Fallen_Order "Star Wars Jedi: Fallen Order")*. *Fallen Order* takes place five years after the [Great Jedi Purge](/wiki/Great_Jedi_Purge "Great Jedi Purge"), which is dated to 19 BBY by *Star Wars: Galactic Atlas*. Therefore, *Star Wars Jedi: Fallen Order* is also set in 14 BBY. As *Darth Vader: Dark Lord of the Sith 18* is between both *Tarkin* and *Darth Vader: Dark Lord of the Sith 19*, the events of the issue must take place in 14 BBY. Since [*Darth Vader* (2017) 20](/wiki/Darth_Vader_(2017)_20 "Darth Vader (2017) 20") takes places immediately after the 19th issue, the events of this issue must also take place in 14 BBY. 106. ↑ [106.0](#cite_ref-The_Lost_Commanders_106-0) [106.1](#cite_ref-The_Lost_Commanders_106-1) [106.2](#cite_ref-The_Lost_Commanders_106-2) [Rebels-mini-logo](/wiki/Star_Wars_Rebels "Star Wars Rebels") *[Star Wars Rebels](/wiki/Star_Wars_Rebels "Star Wars Rebels")* — "[The Lost Commanders](/wiki/The_Lost_Commanders "The Lost Commanders")" 107. [↑](#cite_ref-DC-15_124-0) *[Star Wars: Absolutely Everything You Need to Know](/wiki/Star_Wars:_Absolutely_Everything_You_Need_to_Know "Star Wars: Absolutely Everything You Need to Know")* states that the [DC-15A blaster carbine](/wiki/DC-15A_blaster_carbine "DC-15A blaster carbine") inspired the [E-10 blaster rifle](/wiki/E-10_blaster_rifle "E-10 blaster rifle"), and [StarWars-DatabankII](/wiki/Databank_(2014-) "Databank (2014-)") [E-10 Blaster Rifle](https://www.starwars.com/databank/e-10-blaster-rifle) in the [Databank](/wiki/Databank_(2014-) "Databank (2014-)") ([backup link](https://web.archive.org/web/20190910060340/https://www.starwars.com/databank/e-10-blaster-rifle)) states that the E-11 medium blaster rifle was the successor to the E-10. Therefore, the DC-15 ultimately inspired the E-11. 125.
